Shanghai Tramways Company: All Conductors Indignant Because Zhu Huiren Was Dismissed Innocently; Request for Reinstatement Unsuccessful After Petition 101

According to the Dagong News Agency, more than 450 conductors of the Shanghai Tramways Company are indignant because conductor No. 330, Zhu Huiren, was falsely accused by inspector No. 127, who fabricated facts and reported them to the company. The company authorities did not investigate the truth and unreasonably dismissed him, causing him to lose his livelihood and attempt suicide by drowning in the river. Fortunately, he was rescued. All the conductors were dissatisfied after hearing this and jointly petitioned the company's general manager, Irvine, requesting relief. Yesterday, they sent representatives to request it, but were also rejected, causing indignation among all the conductors. The details are recorded below:

Petition for Reinstatement

Zhu Huiren, conductor No. 330 of the Shanghai Tramways Company, has been working for the company for more than ten years. At 9:30 p.m. on the 3rd of this month, he was working on the No. 8 tram. When the tram arrived at the gate of the Tongxing Cotton Mill in Yangshupu, seven mechanics boarded the tram. Because one of them accidentally injured his finger on the iron gate, the conductor comforted him, which prevented him from selling tickets. When a Chinese ticket inspector, No. 127, boarded the tram to check tickets, he believed that the conductor was suspected of skimming money and reported it to the company. However, the company did not investigate the truth and immediately dismissed him, causing him to be unjustly accused and have no means of living. He attempted suicide by drowning in the Suzhou River and was fortunately rescued by the water patrol team. All the conductors of the company heard the news and jointly submitted a petition to the company, requesting that the dismissal order be revoked, but it was not approved. Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., they sent four representatives to the traffic superintendent, Pollock, requesting permission to be reinstated in order to maintain their livelihood, but were also rejected. All the conductors were panicked after hearing the news and decided to ask the company for reinstatement again. If they do not achieve their goal, they will take effective action to help him.

Letter to the Company

The conductors of the company jointly submitted a letter to Irvine, the general manager of the Shanghai Tramways Company, stating that inspector No. 127 fabricated facts and made false accusations, causing conductor No. 330 to suffer an unjust wrong. They requested a detailed investigation, revocation of the order, and reconsideration in order to redress the grievance and appease public anger. Conductor No. 230 has been serving the company for 16 years, has been diligent in his work, and has spent his youthful energy in these 16 years. Now, because of a trivial matter, without careful investigation and listening to one side of the story, his job was suddenly terminated, causing his family to have nothing to rely on, and he is bound to face the tragedy of his mother dying, his wife leaving, his children scattering, and suicide. How violent is the company's approach to dealing with workers? According to No. 330, at about 9:30 p.m. on the 3rd, seven mechanics came to the tram at the Tongxing Mill stop in Yangshupu. One of them injured his finger on the iron gate, causing an argument with the conductor, which hindered ticket sales. In the short time of one minute, the tram arrived at the Yitai Mill, and there were still four 18-cent tickets that had not been sold. Inspector No. 127 boarded the tram with seven or eight passengers. No. 330 immediately stated to No. 1117 that these seven people had come from the Tongxing small station, and the argument with one passenger had hindered work. Unexpectedly, No. 127 used his position to take revenge and fabricated that ten passengers had not had tickets sold to them. In theory, for all tickets that have not been sold, it is most important to first investigate whether it is possible to skim money. If the tickets are 6, 8, or 10 cents, the inspector should pull them from the conductor and make a report with evidence. If the tickets are 14, 16, or 18 cents, the conductor cannot skim money. The four passengers mentioned above were going to Yangjinghong with 18-cent tickets. Not only could they not skim money at the Yitai Mill, but they also could not skim money at Sanxin or Yangshupu Bridge. Only a person with a mental illness would skim money on an 18-cent ticket. Moreover, No. 330 is an old conductor, how could he dare to take this risk? With a little thought, it can be concluded that the report of No. 127 is untrue. As for No. 127's intentional false accusation of No. 330, the following situation exists: Inspector No. 127 specializes in asking conductors for money. No. 330 has paid bribes many times, even once in February this year, as the diary can prove. According to company rules, if a conductor gives money to a ticket inspector, the conductor may also be dismissed. Therefore, the ticket inspector repeatedly asked the conductor for money, and the conductor dared not report it and could not refuse, because once he refused, he would be in danger of being falsely accused. No. 330 was unjustly accused because he refused. If this matter is not investigated and a fair judgment is not made, listening to a blank document is tantamount to the company authorities creating opportunities for ticket inspectors to ask for money. If the ticket inspector's wishes are not fulfilled, everyone is in danger of being falsely accused and losing their jobs. We are all uneasy and restless. Therefore, we request the company authorities to restore No. 330's work and cancel the unproven report in order to redress the grievance and fulfill the expectations of the public. We are waiting for orders with utmost urgency. Respectfully submitted.

Shanghai West District: Labor Unrest in Japanese Factories Not Expected to Spread; Sixth Factory of Naigaiwata Cotton Mill Resumed Work Last Night; Factories in Shanghai East District Have All Resumed Work; Japanese Side Thanks the Municipal Government for Its Good Intentions in Mediation 102

According to the Dagong News Agency, workers at the Sixth Factory of Naigaiwata Cotton Mill in the Shanghai West District resumed work last night. The remaining factories are consulting directly with the labor side to prevent labor unrest, which is not expected to spread. Factories in the Shanghai East District have all resumed work. Funatsu, chairman of the Japanese Cotton Spinning Association, thanked the municipal government for its assistance in quelling the labor unrest. The details are recorded below:

Sixth Factory Resumed Work Last Night

The overall strike at the Sixth Factory of Naigaiwata Cotton Mill in the West Suzhou Road was caused by a local dispute in which a Japanese foreman beat a female worker in the fine yarn room. It has been going on for two days. The factory's foreman, Nakano Kajiro, spoke with the foremen and supervisors of each class and department yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. As a result, it was decided that wages would be increased after the factories decided on a method, and the dispute over the beating of the female worker would be dealt with after the facts were clarified. Therefore, all workers have resumed work in the night shift yesterday.

Direct Negotiations in Various Factories

After the workers of more than ten factories in the Shanghai West District, including the Japanese Naigaiwata Cotton Mill, Kiwa, Toyota, Nichihua, and Tongxing First Factory, jointly proposed various conditions such as increased wages, bonuses, and rest, the factories are now trying to avoid the occurrence of similar labor unrest, because they have learned that the factories in the Shanghai East District suffered losses after the strike. In addition to advising all workers to wait patiently for a solution, they are also consulting directly with the foremen and worker representatives, and are increasing wages by 5% according to the methods of the Shanghai and other factories. Based on the current situation, the labor unrest in the factories in the Shanghai West District is not expected to spread.

Inspections of Factories in Shanghai East District

Since the party and government agencies sent personnel to mediate the labor unrest in the Shanghai First, Second, Third, Fourth, Fifth, and Sixth Factories, Tongxing First Factory, Dakang, Donghua, Gongda Second Factory, and other factories in the Shanghai East District, they reluctantly returned to work on the 3rd. The reporter of the Dagong News Agency drove to the factories yesterday morning to inspect the situation. The number of workers returning to work has increased compared to the previous day, and the atmosphere has eased. All the detectives stationed in each factory by the police have also been withdrawn.

Japanese Side Thanks the Municipal Government

After the labor unrest occurred in the Japanese cotton mills in Shanghai and other places, the municipal government authorities advised the workers to resume work and wait patiently for a solution. They also sent personnel to visit Funatsu, chairman of the Japanese Cotton Spinning Association in China, to negotiate the five demands put forward by the labor side. Now that the problem of resuming work has been resolved, Funatsu Tatsuiro, chairman of the association, sent a telegram to Wang Xianqing, director of the Mediation Section of the Third Department of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, expressing his gratitude to our government for its mediation and resolution of the labor unrest, and hoped that it would provide assistance at any time to eliminate disputes.

Investigating the Losses of Both Sides

The Japanese Cotton Spinning Association in China, in order to clarify the total amount of losses suffered by the cotton mills in Shanghai and other places that have experienced strikes, has sent Minami Chuzo and others to visit the factories to investigate and inform each cotton mill to report the losses during the strike period. The Shanghai General Labor Union is also conducting a detailed investigation of the losses suffered by the workers through its investigation section.

Huamei Scheduled to Resume Work

More than 120 male and female workers at the Japanese Huamei Printing and Dyeing Factory at 595 Hejian Road in the Shanghai East District went on strike on the 10th of this month because the factory refused to accept the five conditions they had proposed, such as increased wages. Yesterday, the factory owner, Fukuzo, a Japanese, met with all the workers and, as a result of negotiations, agreed to increase wages by two cents across the board. The remaining conditions will be discussed further after work resumes. Both sides have agreed, so the factory workers have decided to resume work on the 16th of this month.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company: Both Freight and Passenger Transport Increased Sharply 103

The state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's business declined and its income was meager in previous years. Since the reorganization this spring, the result of the rectification has been a sharp increase in freight and passenger transport. It is estimated that freight and passenger transport revenue in July increased by more than 11% compared to the same period last year, and in August increased by 48% compared to the same period last year. This has been recorded in various newspapers. It is now learned that the passenger and freight revenue of the company in September this year was 914,119 yuan, 8 jiao, and 3 fen, while the revenue in the same period last year was 589,670 yuan and 5 jiao, an increase of 55% over the total revenue in the same period last year. The revenue in July and August was also higher than previous months. This is not only the result of the company's reorganization, but also a manifestation of the public's support for national shipping, and a precursor to the revival of the entire shipping industry.

Long-Distance Telephone Business Regulations Revised by the Ministry of Communications; Effective Next Month 104

The "Long-Distance Telephone Business Regulations" promulgated by the Ministry of Communications in June 1933 were no longer perfect according to the current business situation. Therefore, a new "Domestic Long-Distance Telephone Business Regulations" was formulated, along with a "Domestic Long-Distance Telephone Classification Price Comparison Table" to calculate various telephone charges. It is said that there are many differences between the new regulations and the old regulations. For example, for calling a person by telephone, the caller was required to pay a special fee in addition to the telephone charge under the old regulations. The new regulations have cancelled the special fee, and the calling-a-person telephone and the direct-dialing telephone are charged the same fee. The scope of calling-a-person is limited to 3 kilometers from the bureau. Other details about various telephone procedures, types of calls, and other names are described in detail in the regulations. The aforementioned new regulations have been circulated to all bureaus by the Ministry of Communications and will be implemented starting on December 1 of this year.

Unified Control of Food - Preliminary Measures Proposed 105

This year's agricultural production is abundant. Although unscrupulous merchants previously engaged in large-scale purchasing of rice and grain in Shanghai and inland areas, leading to price increases, the authorities in rice-producing regions strictly prohibited this. Local grain merchants also voluntarily ceased exports. Consequently, food market prices gradually stabilized. In recent days, the market prices of flour and wheat once plummeted. Although there has been a recent rebound, it is not as intense as the previous price surge. The rice market has been declining in recent days, with the highest price being only around ten yuan. However, with the new harvest coming to market, the falling rice prices will affect farmers' economy. Therefore, the authorities will begin by having local areas compile statistics on food production and sales as a preliminary measure for unified food control. A specific plan will first be discussed by the central government, and then relevant authorities from various provinces and cities, as well as leading grain merchants, will be convened for thorough consultation. Afterwards, measures will be implemented step by step to achieve unified effectiveness.

Agricultural Products Extremely Congested on Jinpu Railway Southbound Trains - Urging Consignees to Pick Up Goods Promptly 106

Agricultural products southbound from the Jinpu Railway at the Makeng Road Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway are extremely congested. The original warehouses are insufficient. Although temporary sheds were added, they were quickly filled. It was necessary to request approval from the Ministry of Railways to shorten the free storage period for arriving goods from five days to three days, so that goods arriving earlier could be picked up promptly to make room for later arrivals. However, it is still impossible to get merchants to pick up goods quickly. As a result, subsequent arrivals cannot be unloaded, and goods still in the rear cannot be transported, greatly hindering the circulation of inland agricultural products. Therefore, another request was made to the Ministry of Railways to charge storage fees for fourth-class and lower goods according to the regulations of 1933 (i.e., 5 fen of national currency per ton per day for carload lots, and 5 li per 25 kilograms for less-than-carload lots). It is hoped that all consignees will pick up their goods promptly to facilitate circulation.

A Brazen Robbery Occurred Last Night in Tongde Lane, Fuxi Road - A Severely Wounded Thief Apprehended - Zhuang Zhiyang's Home Suddenly Robbed - Five Thieves Acting as Lookouts and Searching - Deputy Inspector and Others Bravely Injured - Four Thieves Apprehended and Sent to Hospital 108

At around 6 p.m. yesterday, a robbery occurred in Lane 223, Fuxu Road, in the French Concession. Upon receiving the report, the police dispatched a large number of Chinese and foreign detectives to surround and capture the robbers. The robbers fiercely resisted, and both sides exchanged gunfire. As a result, three robbers were shot and captured. Another robber, having sustained three gunshot wounds, had fled to the Labor Hospital on Xiaoshadu Road for treatment. The hospital notified the police, and he was also apprehended. The duty officer leading the police, Deputy Inspector Pancrazi, and two Vietnamese policemen, No. 486, were injured by gunfire while bravely pursuing the robbers. Details are recorded below.

Iron Gates Between Two Lanes

Lane 223, Fuxu Road, is Tongde Lane. It is located west of Bierre Road and east of Juxiangda Road. The entrance to the lane is extremely narrow. About 100 paces into the lane, there are more than ten newly built shikumen houses. The lane connects to Taihe Lane on Bierre Road to the east. There is an iron gate between the two lanes, which is locked all year round and rarely opened. It connects to Yuyang Lane on Pushi Road to the west, with unobstructed passage between them.

The Zhuang Family's Residence

The first house on the east side of the lane, facing south, is No. 16, a three-story detached house. The sub-tenant is Zhuang Zhiyang from Chaozhou (29 years old). Zhuang is currently a compradore in the export department of Dumou Foreign Firm on Hankou Road in the Public Concession. There are many people in the family. Zhuang's entire family lives on the second floor and in the hall downstairs, while the third floor is rented to Sun Yirong from Ningbo, who is currently working in the coffee export department of Taixing Foreign Firm.

Five Thieves Arrive

At 6:15 p.m. yesterday, while a maid was tidying up in the kitchen of the Zhuang residence, three robbers suddenly broke in through the back door: one wearing a blue cloth short jacket, one wearing a gray robe, and one wearing a striped cloth short shirt. Speaking in the local dialect, the three robbers entered the hall on the pretext of asking for someone named Wang. Two other robbers were acting as lookouts at the door. At the time, Zhuang's younger brother, Zhuang Mingfu, was sitting idly in the hall. One of the robbers wearing a blue cloth short jacket immediately pulled out a handgun, forbade him from making any noise, and forced him into the small room in the back hall.

Monitoring the Family

At the same time, one of the two robbers acting as lookouts at the door entered and monitored Zhuang's brother's movements. The three robbers who had entered together went upstairs and drove all the members of the household, totaling more than twenty people, downstairs and confined them in one place with Zhuang's brother. Then, they went upstairs again and began searching. Unexpectedly, when the three robbers entered the hall and showed their handguns, Zhuang Zhiyang's wife's younger brother, Hu Shaohua, who was only twelve years old and quite alert,

A Young Boy Captured

At the time, Hu saw a robber pointing a handgun at Zhuang Mingfu and knew they were not good people. He first scurried upstairs. The three robbers did not pay attention in the confusion. Hu went up to the third floor, crossed the drying terrace to the adjacent house at No. 17, and exited through the front door of No. 17. He passed through Yuyang Lane and ran to the intersection of Pushi Road and Bierre Road to report to the patrol officer there. Upon receiving the report, the patrol officer immediately reported to the Songshan Road Police Station. The police chief immediately dispatched the reserve team leader, Mei Yi, to rush to the scene first, and then telephoned the Lujiiawan General Police Station to request assistance.

Police Arrive Together

Upon receiving the report, the Lujiiawan Police Station immediately dispatched the duty officer, Deputy Inspector Pancrazi, together with Russian detective S. Taixi Gu, and the general reserve and Chinese and foreign detectives, to rush to the scene. They first surrounded the lane from the outside, then broke down the back door. At the time, one of the robbers monitoring the people downstairs knew things were not good and shouted loudly upstairs. The three robbers rushed downstairs, all planning to open the front door and escape.

Mutual Assault and Severe Wounding

Unexpectedly, the detectives outside the front door had long been lying in ambush on all sides. The two robbers who came out first were seen by the detectives hidden at the door of No. 17 next door, who quickly fired several shots. Both robbers fell to the ground. The two robbers at the rear then fired their guns from inside the door and rushed out. Bullets flew like locusts. The detectives also bravely returned fire, and the two sides exchanged dozens of shots. Deputy Inspector Pancrazi, in particular, charged forward regardless of his safety. The melee lasted for a quarter of an hour. As a result, three robbers were injured and captured. Pancrazi and Vietnamese policeman No. 486 were also shot in the left leg.

The Wounded Sent to Hospital

After the three robbers were wounded and captured, two other robbers escaped. The detectives searched all the lanes but found no trace of them. They took the three robbers back to the police station. After strict interrogation by the police chief, it was learned that one was Gu Rongsheng, 27 years old, one was Wang Rongsheng, 20 years old, and one was Yang Silin, 43 years old. All admitted to conspiring to rob. The three robbers were all wounded in the abdomen and were taken to the Guangci Hospital on Jin Shenfu Road, along with Deputy Inspector Pancrazi and Vietnamese policeman No. 486.

Unexpectedly, while the French police were handling the aftermath, they suddenly received a telephone call from the Public Concession police station, stating that the Labor Hospital on Xiaoshadu Road had just reported that a young boy with three gunshot wounds had come to seek treatment. The hospital, because it was a gunshot wound, specifically notified the police to inquire whether there had been a shooting incident in the French Concession. Upon hearing the news, the French police immediately ordered detectives to rush to the scene. After interrogation, it was learned that he was one of the five robbers who resisted arrest. He was transferred to the French police station. He claimed to be Wang Aiqing, 42 years old, from Jiangyin. The robe worn by the robber was stolen from the Zhuang family. Seeing that the robber was seriously injured, the police chief first sent him to Guangci Hospital.

Cooperation with the People

Afterwards, according to the victim's statement, in addition to the Zhuang family being robbed of more than one hundred yuan and a gold diamond ring, the tenant on the third floor, Sun Yirong, also had a leather bag stolen, containing 34 yuan, as well as a pair of gold earrings. However, some of the stolen goods were recovered from the robbers. Therefore, the actual loss was minimal. The Great American Evening News says that Mr. Hai Caiwei, 23 years old, from Los Angeles, USA, took the road from India to Central Asia to China last year. He suddenly disappeared on the way. For a time, relatives and friends and American consular officials were worried about his safety. Recently, he arrived in Beiping from Guihua, and the world knew that he had trekked through Xinjiang and Mongolia to North China. Now he has arrived in Shanghai by train from Beiping and is staying with his friend Melvin, who came to Shanghai from Los Angeles to find him. The two will soon leave for Los Angeles. Hai's mother is a writer and deeply misses her son. Seeing her beloved son returning home after enduring many dangers, she will be overjoyed. When Hai arrived in Guihua, he ran out of travel expenses and borrowed money to get to Beiping. After arriving in Shanghai, he did not describe the hardships he had experienced on the journey. It is said that he plans to write a manuscript and sell it to an American newspaper to compensate for his losses on the way. According to Hai, he left the United States a year ago and arrived in Bombay in November. He then went to Johor and found a short-term job making a film. In January of this year, he arrived in Beixiawa and took the road to Srinagar, crossing the mountain pass in winter, almost losing his life. While living in Srinagar, he converted to Islam. It is now known that after Hai arrived in Dihua, the Russian officials there suspected him of being a spy and imprisoned him. He was imprisoned for 116 days and tortured in prison, wanting to force him to confess. Hai then went on a hunger strike to resist. Finally, with the intercession of Russian officials elsewhere, he was released. His money, luggage, films, and notebooks were confiscated, and he was only given travel expenses to leave the Xinjiang border. Hai then arrived in Hami. He probably took a car from the Xinsui Automobile Transportation Company from there to Guihua. His experiences could make a great adventure travelogue. It is said that Hai plans to ask the Moscow authorities to instruct the Russian officials in Dihua to return the confiscated items.

Body of Man Bound with Hemp Rope - Conspiracy to Murder 111

Yesterday at around 5 a.m., the body of a murdered young man was found in Xiaobin Nei, east of Tiedi Bridge in Pudong. The upper body was wearing a blue cloth short shirt, the lower body was naked without trousers, barefoot, with a flat-top haircut, about thirteen or fourteen years old. After being discovered by farmers, it immediately caused a sensation in the surrounding area, and many onlookers gathered. Chief Zhang of the Pudong Branch Bureau sent personnel to investigate. The body was pulled to the shore. It was found that the deceased's whole body was bound with hemp rope, six turns around the neck, two turns around the mouth, five or six turns around both hands, and three turns around both feet. It was believed that he had been tightly bound alive and thrown into the river. At the time, the deceased was unable to call for help or struggle and drowned. Therefore, the body was already swollen. The local baozhang was notified to report to the local court. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Tang was commissioned to go to Pudong to examine the body. When the rope was untied, deep rope marks were revealed, confirming that he had been murdered. No relatives of the deceased were found to claim the body. It was ordered to be handed over to the charity for collection and burial, pending the arrest of the murderer.

Li Lili Defrauded - Greek Woman Tells Fortunes and Swindles Money - How Can Fortune Telling Use Gold Bracelets for Longevity? - Court Sentences to Thirty Days of Detention 114

Li Lili, a local woman, 28 years old, who is proficient in English, runs an apartment at No. 15 Jingan Villa on Jingan Temple Road. In June of this year, a Greek woman, Pavlena Stanesko, came to the apartment and said that she could tell people's fortunes with playing cards, and that she was extremely accurate. At that time, Li asked her to calculate for a fee of one yuan. Pavlena then flattered her with flowery words, eventually causing Li to fall into her trap. Pavlena then took the opportunity to say that if she wanted to make her destiny prosperous, she must offer a piece of gold jewelry to the gods, but that the item would be returned after a week. At that time, Li immediately handed over a gold ring inlaid with gemstones to Pavlena to ask the gods for help. Pavlena refused to accept it because the ring was not pure gold. Li then handed over a gold bracelet (worth about 50 yuan) worn on her arm to Pavlena. Unexpectedly, Pavlena never came again after a week, and her whereabouts have been unknown ever since. The police station lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, explained the previous situation and prosecuted her for fraud under Article 339 of the Criminal Code, claiming that the gold bracelet had been sold by the defendant to a Russian woman for about 14 or 15 yuan. Li Lili then gave evidence. Interrogated, Pavlena confessed that Li had repeatedly asked me to tell her fortune in the summer, asking if she would succeed in loving an American man and get married. At that time, the results of my calculations made Li very satisfied, and she also ordered me to tell the fortunes of the residents of her apartment, with all the fortune-telling money being paid to her. Later, she gave me a gold bracelet as a gift. When I met her on Xiafei Road last time, she claimed that she could not achieve the purpose I had calculated, so she wanted to ask for the bracelet back. The bracelet was actually given to me by her, not obtained by trickery. After Judge Ye Shengchao verified the confession, he immediately announced the verdict in court, sentencing Pavlena to 30 days of detention to serve as a warning.

She was already engaged but not yet married. She came to Shanghai to work as a helper. She had a sister-in-law, Zhou Wang, who worked as a helper at No. 8 Hongyun Lane on Kaizi Er Road in the French Concession. However, she did not know the man Wang A Gen who opened the room with the deceased, and did not know who he was. The police station reported to Prosecutor Wang Ren of the Special Second Court, who, along with a forensic doctor and clerk, came to examine the body at noon. The deceased's sister-in-law, Zhou Wang, had not yet arrived. The official questioned the hotel waiter Ding Ziwen and learned that Zhou had committed suicide by poisoning. The body was handed over to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for collection and burial, and relatives were summoned to claim it. Whether the defendant Wang A Gen had instigated or helped suicide was ordered to be investigated and dealt with by the police department. Four opium boxes with a small amount of opium were confiscated by the court. In the afternoon, the deceased's sister-in-law Zhou Wang arrived at the examination site and identified the body. She said that the deceased had dinner at her home on the 11th night and then went out, saying she was going to Ximen Road. She did not know the reason for her suicide. The French police are currently investigating the fugitive Wang A Gen in order to understand the truth about the deceased's suicide.

Hua Jisheng and His Son - Plotting to Harm Hua Liusheng for His Property - First Chopped Off His Leg Bones - The Injury Relapsed and He Died 117

Hua Liusheng, 57 years old, a local, lived with his brother Jifang (also known as Axiang, 62 years old) in Zhujiazhai on Bairinan Road in West Shanghai, making a living by farming. The ancestral land had already been divided and each had established their own household. Jifang had two sons, the eldest named Jinting and the youngest named Baoxing. Seeing that his uncle Liusheng had no children, he planned to seize the property and had repeatedly tried to harm him. On the evening of June 1 of this year, Jifang and his two sons used a kitchen knife and bamboo shoot shovel to chop off Liusheng's leg bones in the dark, and his whole body was also injured by knives. Liusheng shouted for help, and his neighbors arrested Jifang and his youngest son Baoxing and sent them to the Caojiadu Public Security Branch Bureau, who transferred them to the General Bureau. The local court sentenced the father and son to one year of imprisonment each. Jifang and others refused to accept the sentence and are currently appealing. In the meantime, they were released on bail. Liu Sheng's chopped leg bones recently relapsed and became seriously injured. Although he was sent to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment, it was ineffective. He died yesterday morning. His family reported to the Public Security Branch Bureau in charge, and Axiang and Baoyu were arrested. The local baozhang of the Fourth District requested the court to send personnel to examine the body. Yesterday at around 3 p.m., the prosecutor went to examine the body. Because the internal parts and feet could not be clearly understood without detailed examination, it was ordered to be sent to the Zhenru Forensic Examination Institute for examination next Monday.

County Government Orders to Pay Attention: Drowning Deaths and Floating Corpses on Ferries 118

Ferry operator Luo Agou was preparing to ferry thirty or forty passengers at the Fengxian Tangnan pier at 10:30 AM on October 22nd. While dangerously crossing the Huangpu River towards Minhang, he carelessly raised the sail midstream, causing the entire boat to capsize. The first district water police rescued three people, and about six or seven swam to shore. The rest were lost. In addition to the bodies recovered successively, many are still missing. The Shanghai County Government, upon receiving a telegram from the first district requesting that attention be paid to floating corpses, and also based on a report from the County Public Security Bureau, has telegraphed districts one, two, four, and five along the river to pay attention to floating corpses. If any are discovered and confirmed to be drowning victims, their families should be immediately notified to claim the bodies for coffining and burial.

Miss Li's Abortion: Three Defendants Arrested, Case Concluded. Dai Sanwuzi Denies Everything; Yangzhou 'Big Sister' Confesses 119

Li Qianshi, a woman from Yangzhou, lives at No. 469 Tokyo Road, West Shanghai. Her eighteen-year-old daughter, Li Huazhen, works at the Tongxing Cotton Mill on Macau Road. Dai Sanwuzi (also known as Dai Shishun), a twenty-one-year-old Yangzhou native and owner of the Weiwu Barber Shop at No. 188 Haifang Road, saw Li Huazhen passing by his shop daily. He used deceptive tactics, following her and making suggestive remarks, claiming he was without a wife and wished to marry her. Li, young and naive, fell for his scheme. Starting in February of this year, Dai often accompanied Li to secret rendezvous at the Zhongxing Hotel on Rue Robert, where they indulged in intimacy. Unbeknownst to them, a pregnancy began. By the third month, her belly grew, but for the sake of appearances, she decided to remove the fetus to prevent her mother from finding out. On the 4th of last month, Dai, through his neighbor Chen Xu, nicknamed "Yangzhou Big Sister," asked Gao Shishi, a fifty-year-old Suzhou widow and midwife living in a bungalow at No. 116, South Chengdu Road, to perform an abortion. They agreed on a fee of eight yuan. On the same day, Gao inserted a section of equisetum grass into Li Huazhen's lower body. Three days later, the fetus was expelled. However, Li's condition deteriorated significantly after the abortion, and she sought medical treatment. After many days, her condition did not improve. In a panic, Li Qianshi reported the matter to the police on the 28th of last month. Detective Ye Yushan and an ambulance were dispatched to take Li Huazhen to Guangren Hospital for treatment while secretly investigating all involved parties. Fearing exposure, Dai Sanwuzi and the others fled. The police requested the First Special Court to issue arrest warrants. On the day before yesterday, Detective Ye arrested Dai Sanwuzi, Chen Xu, and Gao Shishi. They were separately detained at the Xinzha Police Station and escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court yesterday morning. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang charged them with abortion under Articles 292 and 290 of the Criminal Code, stating that the defendants had confessed and provided statements while at the police station. Li Huazhen remains ill at Guangren Hospital, and her life may still be in danger. When questioned, Dai Sanwuzi not only denied the abortion but also claimed he did not know Li at all. Chen Xu also denied introducing the abortion. When questioned, Gao Shishi admitted that she was introduced by Chen Xu and used equisetum grass to perform an abortion on Li, receiving eight yuan, without denying anything. Gao hired lawyer Ma Leming for defense. Judge Huang Risheng reviewed the statements and declared the case concluded. The verdict is set for the 21st. All defendants are to remain in custody separately.

Pig Trader Robbery Case: Seven Thieves Sentenced; Gu A'er and Others' False Testimony Results in Suspended Sentences 120

On August 13th at 10:00 AM and September 30th at 5:40 PM this year, Xiang Honggen, an employee of the Ninghe Pig Firm at No. 52 Yuezhou Road, and of the Wusong Shentai Pig Firm, was collecting debts at No. 46, Lane Zhoujiazui, when he was robbed of a total of 1,280 yuan by multiple bandits. After investigation, Huajia Police Station detectives Shao Jingfan and Yao Yuanlong, and officers Ma Bingzhang and Li Yinmin, successively arrested the bandits involved: Yuan Linjiang, Xue A'gen, Zhang Shibao, Zhu Caibao, Wang Liangbao, and those already under investigation (Zhu Pinquan, Wang A'mao, and Zheng Jinsheng, who were involved in the Yuezhou Road robbery). A pistol and three bullets were found at Xue A'gen's home. The police investigation revealed that the gun and bullets were planted by Gu A'er, a resident of No. 5 Yuezhou Road from Changzhou, through Xu A'huan, to frame Yuan Linjiang and Zhang Shibao, because they are all involved in the pig slaughtering business and Gu had a grudge against Xue from a previous dispute over pig purchases. Gu and Xu were arrested and handed over to the First Special District Court. After investigation and trial, they awaited sentencing on record. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhong Qing presided over the Third Criminal Court and ruled as follows: Yuan Linjiang and Zhang Shibao were each sentenced to five years and six months of imprisonment. Zhu Caibao was sentenced to six years. Wang Liangbao, Zhu Pinquan, Wang A'mao, and Zheng Jinsheng were each sentenced to seven years. Gu A'er and Xu A'huan, for jointly intending to cause criminal punishment to others and fabricating evidence, were each sentenced to six months, suspended for two years. Public Works Bureau lawyer Zhang Shizhu claimed that the seized firearm was related to the robbery and fatal shooting of Chen Buzhao, a Siyang native, at No. 70 Yangshupu Road on May 27th last year between 9:45 PM and 10:30 PM. He requested that it be temporarily kept by the police station, which the court approved. Gu A'er and Xu A'huan each posted 1,000 yuan in cash or a bond during the appeal period.

Cattle and Sheep Industry Association Announces a 20% Price Increase on Meat Products, Effective November 16th 125

Due to rising meat prices, the Cattle and Sheep Industry Association issued a notice yesterday stating: "Recently, the supply of cattle, sheep, and foreign white-haired pigs has become scarce, and prices have surged. Our colleagues who sell these meat products are still selling at the original daily prices, resulting in significant losses. If prices are not adjusted according to the purchase prices, it will be impossible to maintain operations. The association held an executive committee meeting on November 5th to discuss the price increase. It was decided that, starting November 16th, the prices of beef, mutton, and foreign white-haired pork will be increased by 20% across the board, based on the original prices. For long-term customers with previously agreed-upon prices, the increase should also be applied accordingly to maintain capital. We hereby inform you and hope you will understand."

Shanghai Branch of Vegetable Oil Factory Starts Extracting Tung Oil, Capacity of 60 Tons Daily 126

The Shanghai branch of the China Vegetable Oil Factory, having acquired oil pressing factories such as Dade, Xin'anli, and Jintai, selected No. 180, Junpu Bureau Road, Dinghai Island, as its factory site. After Factory Director Wu Jinquan reorganized it, it commenced operations on the 28th of last month. Although new tungseeds have entered the market, the quantity is still small, so the work is not intensive. However, large quantities are expected to arrive in the middle of next month. The factory's existing equipment can press 60 tons of tung oil daily. The total tungseed production in Zhejiang Province is approximately 200,000 dan, which can be entirely pressed into tung oil within four months. Zhejiang Province also produces a large amount of wubai, which can be pressed into perilla oil. The factory's perilla oil pressing machine is also being reorganized. The equipment from the other two factories will be dismantled and transported to Hunan and Hubei for installation.

Results of Audit of Sihe Company: Accusation of Embezzlement and Breach of Trust Against Zhang Wendi; Allegations of Various Inflated Expenses and Embezzlement; Defendant Ordered to Submit Written Defense 134

Wu Wuming, a 46-year-old Suzhou native residing at No. 117 Rue Amiral Schwerer in the French Concession, engaged in the business of jade and antique trade. He recently engaged a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the Second Criminal Court of the Special Court, accusing his fellow villager Zhang Wendi, residing next door at No. 119, of embezzlement and breach of trust. According to the lawsuit, the plaintiff, the defendant, and other shareholders invested capital to establish the Huazhen Company in this city to engage in the jade business, with the defendant serving as the manager and the plaintiff serving as the shareholder and chairman of the board. During the Chicago World's Fair in the United States in 1933, Zhang Xianglin and Huazhen Company jointly formed the Sihe Company, and the defendant took jade items to the United States for the fair. After returning to China two years later, the expenses were considerable. In July of last year, the Huazhen Company held a board meeting, and the defendant submitted the income and expenditure accounts from the United States. It was resolved to audit the accounts, but the defendant refused to hand them over. After the plaintiff filed a lawsuit in the Civil Court of this court, the defendant was ordered to hand over the accounts. The defendant handed over eight account books and a small book of income and expenditure accounts from the United States, which were entrusted to accountant Pan Xulun for auditing. The audit revealed seven points of false and incomplete accounting by the defendant, including: inflated commissions of over 12,890 US dollars; inflated jade tax and levies of over 5,450 US dollars; inflated public relations expenses for goods sold of over 1,030 US dollars; inflated entertainment expenses for sales litigation of 250 US dollars; unauthorized payment of public relations fees of 500 US dollars; unauthorized living expenses of 1,000 US dollars; embezzlement of a remaining balance of 634.75 US dollars and 225.76 yuan in national currency from the US fair accounts. The plaintiff requested legal investigation and prosecution. Upon receiving the complaint, the court, presided over by Judge Chen Shuoying, summoned the parties to the Second Criminal Court yesterday. Both parties, accompanied by lawyers, appeared in court. After questioning by the court, it was decided to postpone the hearing to the 25th and ordered the defendant to submit a written defense to the court as soon as possible for review.

Moore Memorial Church: Improved Family Movement Concludes Yesterday 137

Tea Reception Welcomes and Sends Off New and Former Pastors

The Moore Memorial Church on Yuqiaqing Road, formerly following the resolution of the China Christian Council, held an "Improved Family Movement" publicity week starting last Monday. It concluded at 3:00 PM yesterday. More than 500 male and female guests attended. Mrs. Liang Guansong, the chair, reported on the progress of the "Improved Family Movement" publicity week and invited Miss Shen and Miss Li to perform piano solos. The female students of the church's special course sang and performed a drama, "Model Family," which was divided into two acts: infant daily life and child rearing and family education. The performance was particularly brilliant and won much applause. At around 5:00 PM, a tea reception was held to welcome and send off the new and former pastors. Chairman Shi Youhui, representing Moore Memorial Church and Jinglin Church, delivered welcoming and farewell speeches. New Pastor Jiang Changchuan and former Pastor Zhu Guishen responded with thanks. The event concluded with refreshments.

National Cartoonists Association to be Established Soon 138

The First National Cartoon Exhibition, which opened at the Great World (Da Xin) Department Store on the 4th of this month, has been running for twelve days as of today. Daily attendance has been very enthusiastic, and many people from all walks of life have purchased paintings. After the exhibition closes today, the association will entrust all remaining net proceeds, estimated at over 600 national currency units, to a bank for safekeeping. This sum will be used as a foundation for the National Cartoonists Association, specifically to reward and support emerging artists. This will further promote the flourishing of cartoon art. Furthermore, today is the last day of the National Cartoon Exhibition. It will begin at 1:00 PM and officially close at 8:00 PM in the painting hall on the fourth floor of the Great World Department Store. After closing, it will be moved to Nanjing and will not be extended again.

Wang Shaoding Goes to Europe for Investigation 140

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after recent expansion, the Haipu Pharmaceutical Factory's operations are thriving. The factory has specially dispatched Mr. Wang Shaoding to Europe for investigation. Mr. Wang is a graduate of the Sino-French Pharmaceutical School, 24 years old. On November 14th, at 9:30 AM, he boarded the French mail steamer *Far East (Félix Roussel)* to Marseille and then transferred to Lyon to enter the pharmaceutical department of the University of Lyon. It is hoped that upon completion of his studies, he will make great contributions to the factory and benefit society.

Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau's Propaganda Vehicle to Depart 141

"Sweat Money" Film Edited and Finished; To Visit Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian First

Since its establishment, the National Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau has seen its business develop rapidly, with savings amounts nearing 60 million yuan. Although affected by the situation in September, there was a decrease of eight per thousand, but in October, it gradually returned to normal. In order to promote the national savings movement, the bureau has specially built a mobile propaganda vehicle and filmed a propaganda film, "Sweat Money," which will be shown in various places. Yesterday, when a reporter from the *Shen Shi News Agency* interviewed Director Zhang of the bureau, he was informed that the vehicle was ready and the editing of the film was nearing completion. Therefore, the official departure is scheduled for the beginning of next month, first visiting the five provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian, and then covering the entire country.

Porter Gangs Clash with Weapons 142

At the South Pier in Pudong, there are two gangs of porters: one from Anhui and one from Hubei. They specialize in carrying goods on the pier. Yesterday morning around 5:00 AM, a conflict arose over competition for business, leading to a fight. They attacked each other with iron tools and carrying poles. As a result, six workers from the Hubei gang were injured. The Public Security Bureau dispatched police to disperse the crowd and sent the injured to the hospital for treatment. The injured include Zhang Huaji, 50 years old, from Hubei, injured in the waist; Hua Dahe, 16 years old, from Hubei, injured in the buttocks and waist; Zhang Xuanji, 41 years old, from Hubei, injured in the left chest and left shoulder; Wang Songshan, 28 years old, from Hubei, injured in the waist; Yu Guanghua, 36 years old, from Hubei, injured in the left waist and left upper arm; and Liao Kechang, 31 years old, from Hubei, injured in the back of the head and left back.

Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association: Local Goods and National Defense Exhibition 143

In order to promote the country through domestic goods and disseminate knowledge of national defense, the Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association has specifically scheduled today (the 15th) to hold an exhibition of local goods and national defense at the Rixin Elementary School in the town. More than a thousand kinds of goods have been collected from various sectors, including seven major categories: local cloth, local products, toys, daily necessities, air defense, models, and charts. The exhibition will begin at 9:00 AM. Admission tickets have been printed and distributed in advance. It is estimated that 3,000 people will attend today, making for a grand scene. In the afternoon, there will be speeches by celebrities, and in the evening, there will be educational films. This is a valuable undertaking during this period of extraordinary education. It is said that after the exhibition in Gaoqiao, it will be shown on tour in various rural areas to expand publicity.

Jingde Fellow-Countrymen's Association Preparatory Meeting 148

Jingde is located in the mountains of southern Anhui. Recently, it has been affected by natural disasters and man-made calamities, and an increasing number of people have come to Shanghai to make a living. They are scattered throughout Shanghai, without any effort to unite or foster mutual assistance. Although there is an Anhui Fellow-Countrymen's Association, its scope is too broad, and small counties are often neglected. Therefore, fellow-countrymen's associations divided by county are springing up one after another. Fellow countrymen from Jingde, in order to connect emotionally and jointly seek public welfare, have initiated a motion to establish a Jingde Fellow-Countrymen's Association in Shanghai. They have temporarily borrowed the Minzhong School on Xilin Heng Road, Ximen, as the meeting place and have chosen 2:00 PM on November 29th to hold the first preparatory meeting. Fellow countrymen from Jingde are urged to participate at that time.

Volume 2, Issue 1 of *Healthy World* Published 149

*Healthy World* monthly magazine, Volume 2, Issue 1, has been published on schedule. Whether in terms of content, layout, or printing, it is more advanced than Volume 1. The categories have also been increased and enriched. The main topics include: "The Current Health Status of the Chinese People," "Cruel," "Superstitious," "Self-Contradictory Youth Sexual Behavior," "Diet Allocation Problems," "Discussing the Promotion of Sports," "Mass Health Discussion," "Wartime Poisoning Prevention Knowledge," "Hygiene During Girls' Development," "Family Hygiene Lecture," "Bedroom Hygiene and Healthy Sex Education," "Several Winter Hygiene Product Manufacturing Methods," "Prevention and Treatment of Diphtheria," and more than thirty other articles. In addition, there is a finely printed *Healthy World Pictorial* and health cartoons. The general distributor of the magazine is Shanghai Life Bookstore. All major bookstores, magazine companies, and bookstalls in Shanghai and other places are selling it. The retail price is one dime of national currency per copy. Subscriptions can be ordered directly from the general distribution office, *Healthy World* magazine, No. 14, Lane 214, Tongfu Road, Shanghai. A one-year subscription of twelve issues, including postage, is priced at only one yuan domestically.

On November 10th, at 4:00 PM, Police Officer Pan Hanzhang of the Wenmiao Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau found a lost, unnamed girl on Lujiahong Road. Publishing World 151

*International Herald* to Publish Soon

Many progressive writers in China will publish an aggregated *International Herald* bi-monthly, with content designed to meet the needs of the majority of readers, focusing on analyzing current affairs, researching real problems, and introducing all important international treatises. In particular, it will systematically report on the international people's front and the liberation movements of oppressed nations. The journal is hosted by domestic writers, with a well-organized lineup, and the format adopts the newest methods to strive to make this publication a representative reading of the newest inclinations in China's cultural world. The inaugural issue will be published on the 15th of this month.

*Current World*, Issue 7, Published

*Current World* bi-monthly, Issue 7, was published on the 16th of this month. The content of this issue includes many articles with opinions on the Sino-Japanese problem from cultural pioneer Mr. Ma Xiangbo et al., as well as "The Dead End and Way Out of Sino-Japanese Negotiations" by Yu Zhenzhi, and "Japanese Public Opinion on Sino-Japanese Negotiations" by Ji Ming. At this time, when the Sino-Japanese diplomatic situation is at the most critical juncture, it is of great contribution to the Chinese people. This issue of the journal pays special attention to the European issue, with "A General Review of the European Political Situation" by Ge Qiao, "The Secret of France's Maginot Line" by Hu Yisheng, and a translation of "A General Review of the Military Strengths of the Major European Countries." The literary section includes "The Fall of a Giant Star" by Guo Moruo, expressing mourning for Mr. Lu Xun, as well as Shen's description of their past relationship, which is a valuable document for China's cultural world. In addition, there is the long serialized novel *Tsushima*, which describes the naval battles between Japan and Russia in the Sea of Japan during the Russo-Japanese War, which is very moving. The correspondence section includes "Students and Soldiers on the National Defense Front," depicting the situation of students in Beiping visiting the 29th Army's large-scale exercises, and the continued draft of the glorious war history of the Northeast Iron and Blood Army is also published in this issue. In addition to the original columns such as serial comics, mass air defense, youth problem discussion, China and Japan, and the economic life of China in the past half month, this issue also opens up a "Criticism Forum" with three short articles commenting on current affairs. It is reported that the next issue will add the two columns of "Women's World" and "Overseas Chinese Life."

Weather Report 153

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and the surrounding areas are clear and colder, with strong northwest to north winds. The Yellow River basin has southwest to northwest breezes. The upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with fog, and the wind is unstable. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the East China Sea, and Taiwan are clear and cold, with fog and strong northwest to northeast winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 70.0 degrees, and the lowest was 49.1 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 66.2 degrees, and the lowest was 59.4 degrees.

Letter 154

To the Editor:

I am writing to you regarding the news item in today's newspaper under the heading "Chinese Staff Association Holds Meeting Yesterday, Opposes Municipal Council's Staff Cuts and Salary Reductions." The phrase "If there are to be staff cuts and salary reductions, Chinese staff must be treated the same as foreign staff" is inconsistent with the facts. It should be changed to "Improve the existing treatment of Chinese staff and unanimously oppose salary reductions" for correction. I hope you will look into this matter.

Sincerely,

Executive Committee of the Chinese Staff Association of the Shanghai Municipal Council

Overview of Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Changes in July and August This Year (Continued) (Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview 38) Chief Editor, Chinese WeChat 156

B. Related to August

In August, there were five important changes in the financial industry under the special industries category:

1. China Industrial Bank Cuts Two Offices—The bank was prepared by the Ministry of Finance under order in the 4th year of the Republic (1915), and was established in April of the 8th year of the Republic (1919). The fixed capital was 20 million national currency units, and the actual paid-up amount was 3.50704 million yuan. It was a joint-stock company and was specially permitted by the government to issue banknotes. Since its opening, its business has been very good. After the currency system reform last year, the banknotes issued by the bank were ordered to be gradually merged and collected by the Bank of Communications. The prize-winning savings it handled was also transferred to the Central Trust Bureau. Therefore, the original business has been slightly reduced. After the death of the bank's president, Mr. Hu Mengjia, in June of this year, the bank's chairman, Mr. Gong Xianzhou, concurrently took over. Since taking office, Gong has been determined to rectify the situation. Since the Yuyuan Road and Hongkou offices were no longer necessary, they were merged into the Nanjing Road and Beijing Road offices respectively to continue operations.

2. Shanghai Silk Industry Commercial Savings Bank Cuts Branches—The recent reorganization of the bank has been detailed in last month's report. Recently, in order to adjust the business policy and save various expenses, the Hongkou, Western District, and Baxianqiao branches were merged into the head office to handle business. This is also one of the rectification plans of Mr. Lu Zidong, the new general manager of the bank since taking office.

Hard Court Tennis Singles Final: Ma Anquan Wins Championship, Defeats Li Pizu in Straight Sets Yesterday; Today's Doubles: Ma Zhou vs. Li Hu 158

Ma Anquan, the "Allison" of the Chinese tennis world, defeated Li Pizu in straight sets yesterday to win this year's Shanghai French Chamber of Commerce Hard Court Tennis Singles Championship. (Note: Mr. Ma's spirit and posture are very similar to those of the famous American tennis player Allison, hence the name.) Mr. Ma was previously the junior singles champion of the Grass Court Tournament. For several years, there has been no significant progress, but his hitting technique is skilled, and his experience is quite rich. In this hard court tournament, he successively defeated Western players such as Korasha and Canavanlo. It was known early on that he had the highest hopes of winning the title. Li Pizu, the Nanjing champion, came to Shanghai to participate. In the quarter-finals, he eliminated Shen Meizhen, who had defeated Sguia. His skills are also commendable, but due to nervousness and unstable forehand strokes, he was defeated by Ma Anquan. The other match, originally the women's doubles final, was temporarily changed to the singles final. The opponents were Mrs. Klenov and Mrs. Hailey. Both players were skilled and the match was tense. The performance was more intense and exciting than the men's singles. In the end, Mrs. Klenov won the championship with a score of two to one. The results of the two matches are as follows:

Ma vs. Li: Ma Anquan controlled the game with his all-around hitting technique. Li Pizu's backhand was also quite steady, but his forehand was weak and uncertain. He was also somewhat nervous at the beginning of the match, allowing Ma to win five consecutive games and take the first set with a score of six to one. At the beginning of the second set, Li Pizu was able to calm down and respond calmly, so the situation suddenly changed, with a tendency to come from behind. He took the lead with three to one, four to two, and five to four. But at this critical moment, Ma Anquan emerged late and created a six-to-six tie. The subsequent battle became tense. Li Pizu repeatedly tried to make a big move, but failed, and was beaten by Ma with eight to six consecutive wins.

In the third set, Li Pizu suffered a setback from the previous set's near success, and his morale seemed to be somewhat frustrated. Ma Anquan rose sharply, his spirits lifted, and five to zero was again hung high on the scoreboard. In the sixth game, Ma served and was ahead with 40-15. He only needed to add another point to complete the task. Li Pizu made a final struggle, suddenly rising to prominence and breaking Ma's serve. He then won the next game, making the score five to two. But in the end, he failed to reverse the situation and was beaten by Ma with six to two, creating a straight-set result and winning the championship. The two players' battle was slow and lacked highlights.

Women's Final: The women's singles final, before the Ma-Li battle, featured Mrs. Klenov, who was stout and had sharp shots, and Mrs. Hailey, who was like a piece of chewing gum, chasing the ball at the baseline with extraordinary steadiness. The two players' performance was far better than the Ma-Li battle, and the tension and fierce competition made the audience excited and appreciative.

Today's Schedule: Today's final schedule is as follows: (1) Women's Doubles: Mrs. Moore and Mrs. Lam vs. Mrs. Hailey and Miss Massey, starting at 1:30 PM on the third court. (2) Men's Doubles: Ma Anquan and Zhou Guanren vs. Li Guofan and Hu Xuguang, starting at 2:30 PM also on the third court. (3) Mixed Doubles: Mrs. Moore and Mr. DeFou vs. Mr. and Mrs. Klenov, starting at 2:30 PM on the second court.

Novel Maritime Ball Game: American Football Match - St. John's Defeats McTyeire - First Time Tied at Six to Six, Yesterday St. John's Won Decisively 19 to 6 162

The St. John's University football team, the only team to promote American football among foreigners, played against the McTyeire American School team for many years. The students of both schools were very interested, and various cheering squads cheered and supported them on the field to enliven the enthusiastic ball game.

The two teams met for the first time two weeks ago. The two sides were evenly matched and in high spirits. As a result, each scored six points, resulting in a tie. Yesterday, the two teams met again at McTyeire American School. The St. John's team, after intensive training in the past two weeks, made rapid progress in their ball skills. As a result, they defeated McTyeire by a large margin of 19 to 6.

The St. John's team often used surprise tactics to break through the opponent's defense line, and their commands were well-coordinated, leaving the McTyeire team at a loss. The enthusiastic cheers of the McTyeire girls ultimately failed to save their warriors from defeat.

Announcement of the Order of the Billiards Tournament - Team League Starts at the End of the Month - Eight Teams Participate, Junior Group Starts Simultaneously - Group A Starts in January Next Year 163

The Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association officially announced yesterday the order of the five competitions organized by the association. Judging from the joint competition of various associations and the open individual competition, the situation in this tournament is clearly more advanced than before. Our country's billiards king, Li Gongying, is not listed, presumably to increase the interest of the general public in competition. Among them, the junior competition, team competition, and the "Volunteers of America" snooker competition will be held within this year, and the rest will start next year.

Team Competition

Eight teams will participate, with five players per team, each scoring 300 points. A double round-robin system will be adopted, with matches held in each team's billiard room to determine the winner. It will start on the 30th of this month and end on March 21st next year. The list of the eight teams is as follows: Chinese YMCA, Western YMCA, International Recreation Club, Portuguese Club, Shanghai Municipal Council Club, Western Police Recreation Club, Shanghai Volunteer Corps Club, and Race Club Staff Club.

Senior Competition

Ten people will participate, and the Chinese players listed are Zhang Yingda, Wu Yuqi, Ding Mingyi, Zhu Qiliang, and Wu Chengqi. The Portuguese master Medina has also signed up to participate. The competition will start on January 18th next year and end on February 5th. Each match will be won by the first to reach 1,000 points, and the finals will aim for 2,000 points. The competition will be held daily at the Amateur Billiards Association at 88 Nanjing Road.

Junior Competition

Twenty-six people will participate, including nine Chinese players. The rest are mostly British. It has been scheduled to start on the 30th of this month and is expected to end on February 1st next year. The competition will be 500 points per month, and the finals will be 1,000 points. The time is 5:30 PM and 9:00 PM every day, and the location is inside the Amateur Billiards Association.

Snooker Competition

This competition is divided into two types. One is the "Volunteers of America" snooker competition, which starts from December 16th to February 2nd next year, with eleven participants. The other is the snooker competition, with twenty-one participants, which starts on January 4th next year and ends on February 3rd. No Chinese players participated in the above two competitions.

Jointly Organized by the Municipal Stadium and the Municipal Sports Association - The Second "Iron City Cup" Basketball Tournament - Registration Starts Today, Deadline is the 25th - Divided into Men's and Women's Groups A and B, a Total of Four Groups 164

The Shanghai Municipal Sports Association organized the first "Iron City Cup" basketball tournament last winter, which was quite successful. It is now known that this year's competition will be jointly organized by the Municipal Stadium and the Municipal Sports Association. Registration starts today. The competition regulations are as follows: Article 1: This stadium association will hold the second "Iron City Cup" basketball tournament in order to promote amateur sports and improve basketball skills. Article 2: The address of the Shanghai Municipal Sports Association is inside the Shanghai Municipal Stadium. The office of this competition is located in the guidance group of the stadium. Article 3: Any amateur sports organization in this city can participate in the competition if it submits a formal request and passes the review of the association's committee. Article 4: The competition is divided into men's and women's groups A and B. If there are many participating teams in each group, it will be held in separate divisions. Article 5: When registering, each men's team can have up to twelve players, and each women's team can have up to fifteen players, excluding managers and coaches. Article 6: Those who wish to participate in the competition must first obtain a registration form from the office of the guidance group of the Shanghai Municipal Stadium, fill it out in detail, and submit a deposit of five yuan and a recent half-length portrait photo of all team members to the association's office. The association will issue a receipt, and they will become official members. Article 7: Registration starts today and ends on the 25th of this month. Those who register by mail must attach the deposit and photos and send them by registered mail through the post office. Article 8: Each group's competition will adopt a single round-robin system. Article 9: The competition rules will adopt the latest rules approved by the Chinese National Sports Association. Article 10: The referees will be hired by the committee and announced in the city's newspapers one day before the competition. Article 11: The competition venues will be in the gymnasium of the Municipal Stadium. Article 12: The competition time is from 7:00 PM to 10:00 PM from Monday to Friday, from 2:00 PM to 10:00 PM on Saturday, and from 9:00 AM to 10:00 PM on Sunday. Article 13: Each team can indicate the most suitable and absolutely unsuitable times for the competition on the registration form for scheduling purposes. Article 14: The uniforms will be prepared by each team, and the colors must be consistent. The numbers on the uniforms must comply with the basketball rules. Article 15: Each player cannot represent two teams in this competition. Article 16: Once the competition starts, the team members of each team cannot be changed. Article 17: Once the competition schedule is announced, no changes can be requested. If there are special circumstances, changes may be made with the committee's approval and if there are legitimate reasons. Article 18: Teams that fail to arrive at the venue within ten minutes of the scheduled start time of the competition will be considered to have forfeited. If neither side arrives, both will be considered to have forfeited. Article 19: The deposit and photos will be returned after the entire competition is over, but those who forfeit more than two matches midway will have their deposit confiscated. Article 20: If a team has a protest, it should formally submit a written protest to the committee for judgment within 24 hours of the occurrence of the event. All protests must be accompanied by a deposit of five yuan. If the committee believes that the protest has sufficient grounds, the deposit will be returned. Otherwise, it will be confiscated. The committee's decision is final and no further protests will be allowed. Article 21: These regulations will be effective after being approved by the committee and reported to the competent authority for record.

Education News

This City Continues to Run Literacy Education - The Fifth Session of Literacy Schools Has Already Started - The City is Divided into Six Central Areas 170

Shanghai's literacy education has been running for four sessions from August 1st last year to July 31st this year, and the results are remarkable. It is now known that this year's literacy education will continue to be held. The city's fifth session of literacy schools started on the 1st of this month and all schools started classes uniformly on the 10th. The implementation procedure is that the city is divided into six central areas, and each area has a central literacy school, without setting up district offices. This is different from the past. The first central area includes the Hu Nan and Cao Jing administrative districts, with a total of seventeen schools. The central principal is Fu Depei. The second central area includes the Fa Hua, Pu Song, and Zhen Ru administrative districts, with twenty schools. The central principal is Huang Yaohua. The third central area includes the Zhabei, Pengpu, and Jiangwan administrative districts, with twenty-eight schools. The central principal is Feng Xiancheng. The fourth central area includes the Yinhang, Yinxiang, and Wusong districts, with ten schools. The central principal is Xu Bingkun. The fifth central area includes the Gaoqiao, Gaohang, and Lu districts, with five schools. The central principal is Feng Baogen. The sixth central area includes the Yangjing, Yangsi, and Tangqiao districts, with ten schools. The central principal is Zhou Yuanlong. A total of one hundred schools, each school has four classes, each class has a maximum of sixty-five students, each class teaches for one and a half hours divided into two sections, the duration of study is four months, which is one month longer than before, and there is a holiday every Sunday. Each central school district has a model literacy school with five classes, one class is taught by the principal, and the remaining four classes are taught by teachers.

Central Industrial Vocational School - Actively Preparing 171

School Site and Start-up Costs Determined

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 14th) The Ministry of Education established a preparatory committee for the Central Industrial Vocational School to carry out preparations. Initiate the Organization - Secondary School Federation

With Principals as the Organizational Unit

(Shanghai News) Lin Meiyan, Tong Hangbai, Huang Zaoxiong, Chen Jicheng, and other principals from ten schools in this city, including Da Gong Vocational School, Min Li Women's Middle School, Jun Yi Middle School, and Private Shang Zhong, have initiated the organization of the city-wide Secondary School Federation, with the principals of each school as the organizational unit. The initiators are currently carrying out preparations, and the origins are recorded below:

Origins - Shanghai is the hub of Chinese culture, and the education industry is also the most developed in Shanghai. All facilities, whether good or bad, are enough to affect the whole country and the future of the nation. The purpose of education is to improve the past life, grasp the current trend, and create the future culture. Its greatest key should be consistent with the national policy of reviving the nation. We have been engaged in education for decades, or at least more than ten years. We all regard educating young people and transforming society as our lifelong duty, and we all regard reviving the nation as the only guiding principle for education. However, although the goals are the same, the methods may not necessarily be consistent. The reason is that the secondary schools in Shanghai have never had adequate contact. They have no active contribution to the education authorities, and the schools themselves are self-governing and cannot learn from each other's strengths and help each other. Although it is said that different paths lead to the same goal, it is difficult to increase the rate of implementing the education policy. Moreover, the current situation is serious, and the national affairs are in danger. To cope with the environment in extraordinary times, there must be education in extraordinary times. Our responsibilities lie in, we cannot tolerate ignoring, so we organize the Shanghai Secondary School Federation, in order to polish and discuss, so that secondary education can be reasonably rebuilt and developed, which is not only for unity and communication of feelings. Initiators: Lin Meiyan of Da Gong Vocational School, Tong Hangbai of Min Li Women's Middle School, Huang Zaoxiong of Jun Yi Middle School, Chen Jicheng of Private Shanghai Middle School, Zai Manyun of Pudong Middle School, Gu Huayuan of Huahua Middle School, Zhao Shusheng of Minli Middle School, Mai Foru of Zhonghua Vocational School, Feng Yixian of Huben Middle School, and Tao Guangchuan of Jingye Middle School. The mailing address is temporarily located in the Shanghai Education Association, Daji Road, Nanshi, this city.

Commercial News

Yarn and Cotton - Many Parties Taking Advantage of Low Prices - Yarn Market Easy to Rise and Difficult to Fall - Recent Price Increases Intensifying - Prices Close to Spot Yarn 177

The yarn market continues to be strong, and the recent price increases in yarn are intensifying. Many parties are strongly controlling and manipulating the market, and they are also cooperating with Indian merchants in their publicity. Therefore, the market situation in recent months has been quite stable. At the same time, Osaka Sanpin yarn has also risen, so buyers have become more active. Securities and gold industries are providing strong support. However, spot yarn sales are still sluggish. The price of this month's standard yarn is not far from the price of spot yarn.

Standard Yarn Rises More Than Two Yuan Again

The standard yarn market opened this morning, and the near-month momentum was very tight. It was slightly looser when auctioned to the far-month. After the second round, it was heard that Osaka Sanpin yarn had a sharp increase this month, and it was also reported that a long-term company had been organized, and the market situation was strong and gradually rising. However, spot yarn production has not been very smooth. However, many parties buy whenever prices are low, so the market has become easy to rise and difficult to fall. As a result, each month rose by 1.67 yuan compared with the closing price of the previous day. When the market opened in the afternoon, the situation in this month was very strong, and floating households were making up for their positions, and the market price rose slowly. However, spot yarn transactions were sluggish. As a result, this month rose by another 1.3 yuan compared with the morning closing price, and the distant month rose by 0.2 yuan. It was found that Hengsan sold 3,000 bales, Juxing 1,150 bales, Dafeng 1,450 bales, Gengfeng 3,000 bales, Ruida 2,000 bales, Shenji 2,850 bales, Changfeng 2,950 bales, Changji 1,750 bales, Xicheng 1,000 bales, Changyu 700 bales, and Taichang 700 bales.
