The Yarn and Cotton Market After the Shortened Month Period 179

Yarn and Cotton Change Security Deposit - The standard yarn and cotton market of the China Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange has been extremely developed recently. Securities groups and gold groups have joined the yarn and cloth market because their own operations are bleak. Therefore, the auction time has been prolonged. At the same time, the government is cracking down on speculation very hard and has shortened the standard yarn and cotton period from six months to four months. According to market rumors, shortening the period is deeply feared that the number of rounds will increase. Originally, there were four rounds of auctions in the morning and the same in the afternoon for each month, or it may be changed to five or six rounds of auctions. In addition, the security deposit for cotton yarn was originally 800 yuan per hundred pieces, and 300 yuan per hundred dan of cotton. Starting from the 16th of this month, the security deposit for cotton yarn will be increased to 1,000 yuan, and the security deposit for cotton will be increased to 400 yuan.

Weekly Refund of Special Certificates - The China Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange will cancel the special security deposits for the December, January, February, and March cotton yarn starting from the 16th of this month. All special certificates and security deposits that have been paid will be refunded on this day. The November cotton yarn will still be collected at 16 yuan per bale, and the November cotton will still be collected at 6 yuan per dan.

Securities: Bullish Sentiment Seems to Be Emerging; Government Bonds Suddenly Rebound 180

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange saw a sudden rebound in market conditions. However, even though the Suiyuan-Qinghai war has begun and the situation on the Shanxi border is critical, the bulls still exerted their remaining strength to maintain the market, and thus were fortunate enough to avoid a downward trend. However, some bulls took profits and closed their positions, while others were still struggling. Given the current high market prices, future opposition is bound to be quite intense, and the overall situation is difficult to be optimistic about. Looking back at yesterday's trading, at the opening in the morning, bulls in issues such as Nos. 4, 5, and 10 emerged, and there were also many exits from No. 34 (Shanxi issue). Nos. 23 and 47 still saw buying interest. Therefore, the initial price of the current month's Series E bonds was raised by three jiao. However, ultimately, due to strong selling pressure and supply exceeding demand, the bulls were temporarily unable to maintain the market, and the situation suddenly deteriorated, falling by two and a half to seven and a half jiao. In the second session, Nos. 4, 5, and 11 saw further selling, and No. 22 also saw exits, with prices falling by three to six and a half jiao. Later, selling became slightly less active, and the bulls seized the opportunity to push prices up. There was significant buying in Nos. 6 to 6, so prices in the later session rose by three to four jiao again. However, the upward momentum had already weakened. At the opening in the afternoon, the earlier issues resumed their upward trend, and retail investors and No. 32 were seen entering the market again, with Series E bonds rising by three and a half jiao. However, the later issues still lacked momentum, and prices fluctuated up and down. Series A bonds fell slightly by one jiao. The market stabilized by the close, and trading was thin, with price differences ranging from nine fen to one jiao. The final market results showed that Series E and D bonds rose by one and a half to three and a half jiao, while the rest only recovered by a small amount, ranging from five fen to one jiao to three and a half jiao. The total trading volume was 18.11 million yuan. The results of the price increases and decreases are compared and listed on the left (unit: yuan, trading unit: 100 yuan).

American New Cotton Has a Saying About Stopping Management Plans 181

Cotton Speculators Sell Off En Masse

Yesterday, the opening of American cotton futures saw declines of five "bangs" (a unit of weight) to gains of one "bang." Early in the morning, both domestic and foreign long positions were largely liquidated, and cotton farmers engaged in hedging sales, causing a slight drop in market prices. Subsequently, traders and sellers bought in around 11.5 cents, leading to a slight rebound. There was uncertainty in the market, but demand for white cotton remained active, and the domestic situation was strong. Unfortunately, there was no progress abroad, and competition from foreign cotton was also intense. Later, January futures saw limited price buying, and December futures were also driven higher. H. Hester estimated that mill usage this week was 412,000 bales, and Liverpool stocks were 294,000 bales. Before closing, traders bought in, and market conditions turned firm, while hedging sales also increased. Spot prices rose by 5 "bangs," and futures were unchanged to up 9 "bangs." English cotton spot prices fell by 2 points, and futures fell by 3 to 5 points. Indian cotton weakened due to rumors of a halt to the new cotton management plan for American cotton, with speculators and long-time bulls selling off. Flat Goul fell 0.25 to 0.5 rupees, Oomra fell 1.75 to 2.5 rupees, and White Raw Creek fell 1 rupee. The original telegram is to the left. (Dated 13th)

Furthermore, according to a Bombay telegram, the opening forecast for the 14th was White Raw Creek at 116 rupees, up 0.25 rupees; Oomra at 196 rupees, unchanged; and Flat Goul at 157 rupees, unchanged.

Three Types of Yarn and Cotton Rise in Unison 182

Osaka telegram of the 14th: Three types of yarn futures rose by 1.10 to 3.40 yuan, with near-term contracts at 235.80 yuan and far-term contracts at 211.40 yuan. Cotton futures rose by 0.25 to 0.50 yuan, with near-term contracts at 65.30 yuan and far-term contracts at 65.90 yuan.

Finished Cloth and Flannelette Retail Sales Are Particularly Good 183

However, Resale Market for Hand Goods Slips Slightly

Yesterday, the cloth market was agitated by news of estimated cotton production reductions domestically, and market sentiment was tense, with prices trending upward. The Qingdao cotton market for the three types of goods was also favorable. Although current cotton cloth sales were very slow, market momentum remained firm. White shirt flannelette, white twill flannelette, colored plush flannelette, and printed flannelette were selling particularly well in retail shops along the main street. The goods were in short supply. However, due to factories needing to meet deadlines for previously ordered low-priced goods, deliveries increased, causing the resale of hand goods to become inconsistent. Prices generally fell by 0.20 to 0.30 yuan per bolt, depending on the urgency of demand. Tribute cloth, with fewer shipments, commanded higher prices. Serges and broadcloth sales were moderate, and prices were firm due to stable yarn prices. The supply of deeply discounted cotton cloth was already prepared far in advance, but recent transportation issues in the interior have led to sluggish sales and little demand. White goods, coarse cloth, fine cloth, and fine twill are all showing weak demand in the main street. Due to shallow waters, provinces like Hunan and Hubei are trying to ship goods as quickly as possible, and all goods are showing some demand, but only for spot goods. Reports from the Yunnan-Southwest route have been quiet for many days but have now shown some improvement, with shipments mainly consisting of blue cloth, fine cloth, and fine twill.

Crowding Soars by a Yuan 184

With the approach of early winter, there is continued brisk sales of broadcloth and overcoat materials. Retail sales are strong in the Da Xin Street area of the city. The spot wholesale of herringbone, chocolate drill, riding breeches cloth, and crow tops, etc., have seen large volumes traded daily among traders. Among these, crow tops are selling the best. Horse brand cloth has been popular for overcoats for eight or nine years, and chocolate drill has been popular for three or four years. Crow tops were only newly popular last year, and the tendency of customers to prefer the new over the old is inevitable. Sales are currently strong, and imports from both the East and West are significantly lower compared to riding breeches cloth and chocolate drill. Domestic production only includes riding breeches cloth, with no chocolate drill or crow tops. As a result, there is a shortage and prices are soaring. Yesterday, the market saw a sudden jump of more than half a yuan. Western crow tops that sold for 7.70 yuan last week are now being sold for 8.50 yuan by traders. Eastern crow tops that sold for 6.75 yuan yesterday must now be sold for 7.75 yuan, and stocks are extremely low.

Finance: Swap Spread Not Large; Call Money Covers Shorts Actively 185

Although the gold market rose yesterday, buying interest was not strong. Fortunately, the swap spread was very small, and large short positions were actively covered, resulting in a slight increase. The trend is still flat. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets saw England rising and America flat. Traders believed that both buyers and sellers were satisfied after closing, and the market was therefore evenly balanced. Monteree forward silver prices rose by 5 hao to 2.5 li. Exchange rates all rose. London raw gold rose by 1.5 pence. The central bank's listing announcement showed both England and America flat. The customs gold unit rose by 3 li. The standard gold bar price listing rose to 1159.80 yuan. Pre-market trading outside the exchange opened around 54 yuan. Tong Taichang once sold at 3.5 yuan. Hengchang Yong slightly absorbed at lower prices. The morning opening was slightly higher. After the opening, various parties sold slightly, causing prices to fall slightly. However, shorts, aware of the small swap spread, covered their positions, gradually pulling prices up. HSBC's listing announcement showed both England and America flat, and the silver balance tax rose by 1 fen. At this time, large customers were seeking supply, but because most were limited orders, and various firms were focusing on the swap spread, the market was even flatter, with very little movement. The same was true at noon. This swap saw shorts paying 1.90 to 2.50 yuan. After noting the market situation for the first half of the day,

The morning opening was 1153.60 yuan, a slight increase of 0.10 yuan compared to the previous close. Tong Chachang and Fu'an unwound, falling to 3.40 yuan. Chengda, Zhengchang, Fuyu, Dadecheng, and Laijin rose to 3.80 yuan. Qiafeng, Yongwanxing, Tong Taichang, Hengyu, Tongfeng, and Henglai sold, falling again to 3.5 yuan. Dadecheng, Chunyuan, Yongfuxing, and Yongshengyuan absorbed at lower prices. HSBC's listing announcement showed both England and America flat, rising back to 3.80 yuan. Fuxing and Yongshunli, etc., sold off. The silver balance tax rose by 1 fen, gradually declining. The noon close was 1153.60 yuan.

The closing price, based on the central bank's listed standard gold bar price, rose to 1159.80 yuan, effectively pressing down over 6 yuan compared to the closing price. December bars were all priced at 1154 yuan. This month's book entry was 1151 yuan, December 1154 yuan, morning water top-up 1151 yuan. Refined gold was priced up 6 yuan to 1159.60 yuan. The spot market remained stable. Tianjin goods were priced up 13.5 yuan. Refined gold buying price was 10 yuan, all transacted. Selling price was priced up 14.5 yuan, with Dafengheng selling over 100 taels.

Trading within the exchange was generally flat. In summary, Yuanmao Yong, Dadecheng, Chengda, Shengyuan, Yonghengchang, Yongzhengchang, and Chunyuan Yong were on the buying side, while Qiafeng Yong, Tong Taichang, Shenda Yong, Tongfeng Heng, and Wanxing, etc., were on the selling side.

This December swap to January saw shorts initially bidding 2.50 to 3 yuan outside the exchange, but there were no transactions. Qingfayong, etc., then bid, falling back to around 2.50 yuan. Qingfayong, Shengyuan Yong, Dafengheng, Jingfu Qianchang Xiang, and Chunyuan Yong actively bid, but Hengyu and Dachangxiang, etc., although bidding, gradually fell to within 2 yuan. Yuanmao Yong bid for 70 bars from Shengyuan Yong at only 1.90 yuan. Wuchangxiang, Qiafeng Yong, Fuxing Yong, Hengyu, and Yuanmao Yong then bid. When the official opening began at 10 o'clock, longs bid 2 yuan. After opening, although Dadecheng and Qiafeng Yong bid, Wuchangxiang, Yuanmao Yong, Yuanting, and Dachangxiang actively bid, rising to 2.30 to 2.40 yuan. Dadecheng and Shengyuan Yong settled to bid, falling to 2 yuan. Yuanmao Yong, etc., bid. The noon close saw longs bidding 2.10 yuan. Large long positions were unchanged, and the closing price was still pressed. The future may be even flatter.

Checking, the market situation for half a day was calm. The morning opening was 1153.60 yuan, and the noon close was 1153.60 yuan. The highest price was 1153.80 yuan, and the lowest price was 1153.40 yuan, with only 0.40 yuan of fluctuation. The total volume traded for half a day was 7,420 bars.

Among those with outstanding December bars, longs included Qiafeng Yong with over 1,400, Shengyuan Yong with less than 500, Dachangxiang with over 400, Qingfa with over 100, Futai Heng, Yisheng Yongheng, and Fuda each with over 100. Shorts included Dadecheng with over 500, Chunyuan Yong with over 400, Fuxing Yong and Chengda each with over 300, Hengyu and Daheng Jingfu each with over 200, and Runchang Yushun Mao each with over 100, totaling 3,178 bars. There were 8 long parties and 14 short parties.

The new January lineup included longs such as Dachangxiang with over 1,000, Yuanmao Yong with over 800, Wuchangxiang and Qingfayong each with over 400, Yuanheng with over 200, and Fuxing, Lifeng Chunyuan Yong, Fuxing Yong, Fuyu, Xiangfeng each with over 100. Shorts included Shengyuan Yong with over 700, Chengda with over 500, Jingfu and Tong Taichang each with over 400, Yuanchang Yong with less than 400, and Dafengheng and Dadecheng each with over 300, Qiafeng Yong with over 200, and Shunmao with over 100. The total stakes were 4,480 bars. There were 27 long parties and 27 short parties.

Chinese Merchant Congestion in Banks Stabilizes Exchange Market for Half a Day 186

The exchange market yesterday saw continued congestion among Chinese merchants, with banks striving to stabilize the situation. The process finally stabilized. Early in the morning, overseas telegrams reported that London large bars were up 1.875 both near and far, with traders saying that the market stabilized after closing because both buyers and sellers were satisfied. New York silver markets were unchanged. Monteree forward silver prices rose by 9 tai to 2.5 li. London raw gold rose by 1.5 pence. England against America rose by 0.375, England against France rose by 3 pounds, America against England rose by 0.4375, and America against France rose by 0.25. The central bank's listing announcement showed both England and America flat. The customs order unit rose by 3 li. The morning opening of the exchange market saw recent selling prices of English exchange at 1 shilling 2.5625 pence, and American exchange at 29.625 yuan, which was flat for both England and America compared to the previous close, but the American dollar was slightly looser. After the opening, banks actively settled their positions. Although Chinese merchants continued to settle American exchange, HSBC's listing announcement showed both England and America flat, but the market was still tense. Later, the silver balance tax announcement rose by 1 fen, and banks still actively stabilized the market, which began to loosen slightly. The noon close saw recent selling prices of English exchange at 1 shilling 2.5625 pence, and American exchange at 29.625 yuan, which was flat for both England and America compared to the previous close. The forward market was the same. Chinese merchants slightly sold over 100,000 yuan of shillings and American dollars. Now, the recorded transactions are as follows:

Mai Jia Li and Citibank HSBC absorbed March at half a penny. Closing selling price, spot 1 shilling 2.5625 pence, January 2.53125, February half a penny, purchase price negotiable.

Grains: Manufacturers Collect Near and Hedge Far; Flour Futures Rise Near, Fall Far 187

Conduct 192

— Implication

Dear children, your teachers always tell you that a person should not only have good academic performance but also good conduct. Now, let's not talk about academic performance, but conduct. What is conduct? Conduct can be said to be all of a person's behavior. Good conduct can be said to be all good behavior. What kind of behavior is considered good? It is easy to give a definition. We can say that good conduct should be honesty, humility, politeness, and open-mindedness.

What is honesty? Honesty is not deceiving oneself or others. What is humility? Humility is being respectful and polite to others. What is politeness? Politeness is behavior that does not violate rules. What is open-mindedness? Open-mindedness is not being arrogant or conceited.

I have a relative who, after graduating from elementary school, joined a company to learn the trade. In the blink of an eye, his three-year term expired, and he could manage some monetary affairs. However, tempted by his friends, he embezzled company funds. When the matter was discovered, he was fired. He was unable to advance because of his dishonesty. In other words, he was unable to advance because of his poor conduct.

Dear children, academic performance is important, but conduct is also important. The ancients always advised people to "teach conduct and encourage learning," which is indeed correct.

A Little Brother from the Northeast 193

— Wang Shipeng

This time, I brought over thirty children to Nanjing to participate in the National Boy Scout Grand Review. On the first day we arrived in Nanjing, after reporting to headquarters, we began to set up camp at the designated location. It took us most of the day to set up the campsite. We were very happy because tomorrow was the day for people to visit.

The next day, many more people came to visit the camp. Around 2:00 PM, seven young boys wearing Boy Scout uniforms came to visit our camp. After they introduced themselves, we learned that the little boy wearing the black neckerchief was from Jilin, and the other six were from Hebei. They came to Nanjing specifically for the Grand Review. Our thirty-plus children here asked me to urge him to tell us some news from outside the pass.

He said: "My home is in Dunhua, Jilin. After the "Manchukuo" flag was hung on top of our school's flagpole, things changed drastically. Our textbooks also changed, and every school had several foreign teachers. The first lesson in the geography textbook was the borders of "Manchukuo"; the first lesson in the language textbook was the national flag song (referring to the national flag of the puppet state of Manchukuo). Every morning, those teachers came to teach us foreign languages. Usually, the teachers told us that there were many bandits inside the pass, and that everyone was addicted to opium. Only after we came inside the pass did we realize that these words were all lies meant to deceive us.

Studying there was extremely painful. I remember once, a foreign student in our class had a conflict with the class leader for some reason. He reported it to their teacher, and the teacher beat the class leader until he was bruised and bleeding. When the students saw this, who didn't hate it with every fiber of their being? But they all dared to be angry but dared not speak out. My father has always been a businessman outside the pass. Last July, he sent me to my aunt's house in Beiping. I am now studying at the Hebei County Elementary School. This time, coming to Nanjing and seeing the brothers and sisters from all over the country, I am very excited, but every time I think of my school back home, and the many classmates I haven't seen in a long time, I wonder how much injustice they are suffering now?"

He told us this so eloquently that we were all in tears. Because it was getting late, he said goodbye and went back to his camp.

Children, you have all read what this little brother told us, haven't you? Everyone, think about it: what methods can we use to save our brothers and sisters who are in dire straits?

Hope 195

— Hua Ling

I very much hope that China will have such a day:

On a certain day's newspaper, a message is suddenly discovered, printed in large characters, saying that a team of children, all under the age of sixteen, purchased a motorboat three months ago. This motorboat is intended for exploration. Therefore, it is named the "Children's Exploration." All equipment is resistant to huge waves and ice floes. After they had everything ready, they cast off and set sail. Although they are not the world's famous scientists, they all have sufficient scientific knowledge. So driving and radio transmission and reception, etc., are all done by themselves. Since departure, there has been very little news, so there have been repeated rumors that these children have sacrificed in their cause. But last night, this newspaper received a radio report from the "Children's Exploration," stating that "The expedition has already discovered a new continent in the Pacific Ocean, with a very large area that is difficult to estimate at this time. The inhabitants are all aborigines, with very few in number and a simple life. The island is full of metal and oil mines. The team has now raised the national flag and gained sovereignty. It is hoped that the government will quickly send a navy and an aircraft surveying team to work there."

On a certain day's newspaper, a message is suddenly discovered, printed in large characters, saying that in a certain village in its province, there is a fifteen-year-old child named ×××, who was very poor, but he loved to read very much, and even more so to conduct all kinds of modern scientific experiments. When he was eight years old, he already had an ideal of seeking human food from natural substances. For several years, all the income he earned from working for others was completely consumed in his simple and exquisite laboratory. His parents repeatedly obstructed his scientific research, and his neighbors and friends ridiculed his foolishness, but he still persevered in his research. However, countless failures sometimes forced him to cry sadly to himself on quiet nights, but he did not lose heart and continued to work hard. Recently, his research was successful. He discovered a substance in ordinary air that the scientific community has not yet discovered. It can be artificially manufactured into a powdery solid. One millimeter of this powdery solid can replace the nutrients contained in one pound of bread, half a pound of beef, and one pound of milk. It is a very good substitute for food. Even Japanese and foreign reporters and scientists have come to visit and believe that this invention is a great revolution for contemporary politics and economics, benefiting people infinitely. And this year's Nobel Prize in Science will undoubtedly be awarded to this little scientist.

I hope that our Chinese children will have such a day. And at the same time, I believe that our country's talented children will have one day turn my hope into a reality.

Voice 196

— True

One Sunday morning, Min'er and his older brother Ting'er were doing some physical exercises in their garden. The weather was very sunny and clear that day, and the little birds on the branches were chirping. He thought the sound was very pleasant; how could he hear it? He had never doubted this question before. This was a definite reality; what was there to doubt? But now, the more he thought about it, the more questions he had. Once he had a question, he had to solve it, so he had to ask his brother:

"Brother, the singing of the little birds sounds so nice, how can we hear it?"

"If you want to know how to hear the singing of the little birds, you must first know how the little birds make sounds. I say that the sound of the little birds is the vibration of the vocal cords in their throats. It can be seen that the sound is generated by the vibration of an object. How can you know this? I can try to show you." He went to get a pipa, and plucked one of its strings with his finger. The string vibrated quickly and made a clanging sound. Then, he touched the string with his finger, and the vibration of the string stopped immediately, and the sound disappeared as well. He said, "From this, we can know. As for how we can hear the chirping of the little birds? When the little birds are chirping, the surrounding air also vibrates, becoming sparse and dense alternately. This kind of sparse and dense vibration can gradually spread up and down, left and right, and forward and backward, like ripples in water. This is the wave of sound, so it is called a sound wave. When this sound wave reaches our ears and vibrates our eardrums, we feel the sound."

"Brother, why are some sounds loud? Why are some sounds soft? Why are some sounds resonant? What are the differences?"

"The difference between loud and soft sounds is difficult to understand. It is easier to understand if you separate the strength and pitch of the sounds. If the string is plucked harder, the distance of vibration is greater, and the sound is stronger; if the string is plucked lighter, the distance of vibration is smaller, and the sound is weaker. Thus, it can be seen that the strength of the sound is directly proportional to the size of the vibration distance of the sound-producing body. If the string is shorter, thinner, and tighter, the vibration will be faster, and the sound will be higher; if the string is longer, thicker, and looser, the vibration will be slower, and the sound will be lower. It can be seen that the pitch of the sound is due to the speed of vibration of the sound-producing body, that is, due to the number of vibrations. The loudness of the sound is what I call strength, and the sharpness or resonance of the sound is pitch."

"Brother, then why are some sounds pleasant to hear, like the sound of music, and some sounds unpleasant to hear, like crying? What is the reason for this?"

"When a string vibrates regularly, the surrounding air becomes continuously sparse and dense, forming alternating sparse and dense sounds. If the vibration of the string is very regular, the sound produced will naturally be very regular, and we will find it pleasant to hear, so we call it musical sound. The vibration caused by the sound of crying is irregular, so we find it unpleasant to hear, so we call it noise."

Tuberculosis Statistics 197

— Tao

The mortality rate from tuberculosis in China is higher than in any other country, because this germ is most easily transmitted. It is not necessary to have contact with a patient; it can be transmitted unknowingly even in the air. Therefore, the more patients there are, the more opportunities there are to infect others. In the early stage of the disease, it is not easy to detect, but once it is discovered, it is said to have reached the second or third stage. Only then is there a last-minute effort to seek medical treatment, but it is already too late. At the same time, the poverty of the national economy is also a major cause of tuberculosis. Those who are struggling on the line of death, even if they know that they have unfortunately contracted tuberculosis, how can they have the financial means to treat it? Therefore, the tubercle bacillus in China is spreading and expanding day by day, and seems to have formed an inextricable bond with the Chinese people.

Recently, I saw in the newspaper a shocking tuberculosis statistic!

When a certain hospital in this city was conducting an anti-tuberculosis X-ray examination, among the young students who went to the hospital for examination in September, a total of 428 people were examined, of whom 86 had had tuberculosis, 8 had been cured, and 17 were in the early stage of the disease. The total number of patients accounted for about 24 percent. That is, on average, one in every four people is sick. Every child must be chilled to the bone when they see this terrible statistic!

There are many ways to prevent tuberculosis, but the simplest and easiest way is to pay attention to the following items: (1) Pay attention to personal and public hygiene, and promote the implementation of hygiene knowledge among children; (2) Promote physical education and forge a body that is as strong as steel. In this way, the tubercle bacillus will simply be discouraged and unable to invade at all. Only in this way can one's life, which should live to a certain age, not be cut short and not enter the path of "unjust death"!

(3) Little Blackie sees a scary ghost outside the window, and is so scared that he runs away, even forgetting to take the apple on the table.

(4) So the children leisurely come in and eat the apple.

Compass 199

— Wang Ziding

Little friends: You have probably all heard the name compass, right? You probably all know its use too. Here, let me talk about its structure and principle, okay?

Before talking about its structure and principle, we might as well first know its inventor. To put it simply, it was 4,000 years ago, during the time of the Yellow Emperor (Yellow Emperor was his name, his surname was Gongsun). There was a tyrannical prince (Chi You) who rebelled, and the Yellow Emperor sent troops to fight him, but unfortunately, when the Yellow Emperor sent troops, it happened to be foggy for several days, and the Yellow Emperor's soldiers all got lost, so they were defeated.

Soon, the Yellow Emperor invented the south-pointing chariot, which could find directions in the fog. He gave this south-pointing chariot to the soldiers to use, and as a result, he was victorious.

Since the Yellow Emperor invented the south-pointing chariot, later people improved it into the compass. Its structure is very simple. It uses a round plate, with the four characters for east, south, west, and north written on the four corners of the plate. In the center, there is a small column, and a magnetic needle is placed on the top of the column. A piece of glass is placed on the top of the plate, and there is a handle on the right. This is all there is to it.

Now, let's put aside the other unimportant things and just talk about this magnetic needle, because the compass can point south entirely because of this magnetic needle.

What is a magnetic needle? It is a needle containing magnetism. What is magnetism? This is a natural phenomenon, unique to magnetite, which can attract iron parts (iron nails, iron wires, etc.). You have probably all seen magnets, right? If we take a small knife and rub it on it a few times, then this small knife can also attract iron, right? The magnetic needle in the compass is also made using this method. Its two ends are called two poles, one end is the south pole, and the other end is the north pole.

Then how does it always point south? Aren't you curious, little friends? This is very simple. It turns out that the Earth is also a piece of magnet, and it also has north and south poles. The south pole of the compass is attracted by the north pole of the Earth, and the north pole of the compass is attracted by the south pole of the Earth. This is the principle of "opposites attract, and likes repel," so the compass always points south.

The four characters east, south, west, and north in the compass are called the four directions. If you want to make it easier to estimate directions, you can change it to eight or sixteen directions. (The same as eight directions, as above)

The Cricket is Chirping 200

— Rongyu

The Moon Sister wears a round face, showing a cool smile, secretly peeking at the windows of each household. At this time, every child is seduced by her, opening their eyes wide, and refusing to go to the land of dreams for a while. He looks at the window shadow outside the window, reflected on the glass window, and it is actually an excellent sketch. He also hears the weaving maiden hiding in the bushes of the melon trellis. She keeps calling out "Ou! Za!" He can't wait to jump out of bed and take a look under the moon pavilion.

"Qu! Qu! Qu!" Another tempting sound comes from under the steps, and is transmitted very clearly to the pillow. Min'er knows that this is the chirping of the cricket, and associates it with all kinds of things about crickets. He thinks of his neighbor Daxie, who has a strong cricket, and always wins every battle he fights. He also thinks of the cricket's teeth, which are as sharp as weaving pliers; the strength of his legs is just like the driver of a person who is used to running; and the triumphant chirping is as loud as a battle horn. He is lost in thought, and a huge cricket appears before his eyes, as big as a grasshopper. He is still afraid, but the cricket gets bigger and bigger according to his wishes, becoming as big as a cicada in a moment, as big as a frog, as big as a cat, and as big as a dog. Min'er is overjoyed. He thinks that with this cricket, not to mention that Daxie's ever-victorious army next door can't stand half a bite from it, even if all the crickets in the world are gathered together to fight it, it wouldn't care! Min'er also hurriedly follows it. Once in the garden, the big cricket chirps a few times, just like a general giving orders, and thousands of small crickets suddenly emerge from the grass, divided into two teams, glaring and preparing to fight. Another command is given, and the two sides start fighting, with their teeth clenched, their legs kicking, and they fight so excitedly that their bellies are turned to the sky, and they turn over and continue to fight. Once, twice, ... dozens of times, ... hundreds of times, and then gradually the victory or defeat is separated. The defeated side has its abdomen broken and its intestines flowing, and dies stiffly on the ground; even the victorious side has its whiskers broken, its teeth missing, and its legs lame, making moaning sounds. Min'er looks at this situation and feels uncomfortable in his heart, muttering: "They are all our own people, why are they fighting so miserably?" Suddenly, the scene in front of him changes, and the garden becomes a battlefield, and many dead and wounded crickets turn into the wronged souls of dead soldiers. They say in unison: "We don't want to be provoked by others to do such things, we don't want to be puppets fighting our own people, we should unite together to kill the people who provoke the war." While saying this, they point at Min'er and say: "This is our enemy, but he provoked us to fight." As soon as they finish speaking, these many wronged souls, some carrying their severed heads, some with their legs half-broken, some with their bloody intestines flowing, roar and rush towards Min'er, threatening Min'er to pay for their lives. Min'er is taken aback. He wants to turn around and run away, but it is too late. With a cry of "Ah yo," he is covered in cold sweat. He looks and is still in bed, it turns out to be a nightmare.

At this time, Min'er looks at the moonlight outside the window, which is a little hazy; the cricket under the steps is still chirping.

Little Toy Gun 201

— Yang Zhigang

This is a very interesting game: It's very simple, every child can make one himself, and it will definitely be very fun to play with. Now I'll tell you how:

(Tools) One goose feather tube. One thin bamboo stick (about three or four inches long). One piece of sweet potato or similar.

(Method) First cut off the lower section of the goose feather tube (the empty section). Then shave the bamboo stick so that it is slightly smaller than the goose feather tube. Also shave the sweet potato (other melons can also be used) to be about two minutes thick. After these are made, you can start playing! Insert the goose feather tube into the sweet potato, then insert the other end to the bottom, pick it up, and push the bamboo stick into the larger end of the goose feather tube. Then the sweet potato in the goose feather tube will "whoosh" and shoot forward, and can shoot up to two or three zhang away, almost like a toy gun. (See picture)

(Principle) This game completely utilizes the principle of air pressure. Because when you push the bamboo stick into the goose feather tube, the air inside the goose feather tube is compressed very heavily, so it will shoot the sweet potato at the other end outwards!

Filial Piety (4) 202

— Hai

One day, Bois-Corfield was traveling a long distance, not far from a place called Camoggie, when he unfortunately encountered a very violent storm. He hurriedly went forward, hoping to reach the nearest house to take shelter for a while. Unexpectedly, a tree was blown down and lay right in front of him. He thought it would be safer to hide in these dense branches and leaves, at least he would not be blown by the strong wind. When the storm subsided, it was already late. He dared not grope in the dark, so he stayed there, not moving at all. Rainwater dripped from the branches, soaking his clothes. After dawn, he walked back to the road and met a farmer driving a cart, who allowed him to ride in the cart. At eight o'clock he arrived at a village, and the farmer let him off. As soon as he got out of the cart, he fell to the ground. His clothes were not only soaked, but also covered in mud. He was cold, hungry, and exhausted. He looked at the cleanliness of the houses around him, which made him even more surprised, and he dared not approach. However, driven by hunger and cold, he finally mustered up the courage to walk to an open window, where he saw a woman peeling beans. He begged her to let him rest for a while and dry his clothes, but the woman gave him a contemptuous look and told him to leave immediately. He went to another house to beg, and received the same treatment. Then he sat down at the door of a house, but the mistress of the house immediately drove him away, saying that they could not allow thieves and vagrants.

Bois-Corfield thought to himself: No matter what, they wouldn't drive me out if I went to church, would they? But he found the church, only to see that the door was tightly locked. He had no choice but to sit down on the steps to rest for a while. The children in the village gathered around him, surrounding him and shouting at him, calling him a thief and a runaway. He stayed there for two full hours, preparing to freeze to death or starve to death. But he was still praying silently in his heart for God to give him the courage to endure this difficult time.

Finally, a more charitable woman walked up from among the children and spoke to him very kindly. Bois-Corfield told her about his experience of sleeping in the forest in the rain last night. Then the village chief came to check his passport, and found that everything was consistent with his identity. The charitable woman volunteered to take him back with her, but when he stood up, he felt that his limbs were frozen and he could not move. His heels were swollen and he had lost one of his shoes. Sleeping in the wind and rain last night had really caused him great pain. The people in the village also became kind at this time, and brought a cart, carrying Bois-Corfield to go with the good woman. He stayed there for a few days and gradually recovered, seeing that he could travel again. One of the villagers gave him a pair of boots. From then on, he often rested for one or two days, depending on his physical strength, the weather, and the hospitality of the people. Whenever people kept him for a short stay, he often did some small tasks such as sweeping, washing clothes, or sewing to repay them. He felt that it would be wiser not to tell people about his quest to seek forgiveness from his godfather at first, because if he told people, they would think he was a scammer. So he started by just asking people for some food. If the other person was sincere and kind, he would further tell them about his fatigue along the way and beg them to allow him to rest for the night. If the people allowed him to stay, and they talked well with each other, then he would tell them his story from beginning to end.

Celebrity Interview

Uchiyama Bookstore Owner, Kanzo Uchiyama 203

— Xu Xinqin

Before his death, Mr. Lu Xun would often spend his days idly sitting in the Uchiyama Bookstore. This has become common knowledge. Therefore, in the last ten years or so, the Uchiyama Bookstore and its founder, Mr. Kanzo Uchiyama, have been deeply imprinted in people's minds along with the name "Lu Xun." To learn a little about what happened after Mr. Lu Xun's death, and with the intention of meeting Mr. Uchiyama, I arrived at the park shooting range one evening as dusk was settling. After entering the bookstore and asking, I learned that Mr. Uchiyama was out for dinner. A Chinese staff member politely invited me to sit down and wait, and also asked me why I wanted to see him. After I explained that I admired him and was paying a visit, the staff member pointed to a book on the bookshelf titled "A Japanese Person's View of China" and said that it was Mr. Uchiyama's recent work. I saw that there was also an Enlightenment Press Chinese version translated by Mr. Yun Bingqi, and I took the opportunity to pick it up and read it. The first thing I saw was Mr. Lu Xun's preface. In the preface, there were the following introductory remarks: "The author (referring to Mr. Uchiyama) has lived in China for over twenty years, traveled to various places, and come into contact with people from all walks of life. Therefore, I believe he is a suitable person to write such essays. Facts speak louder than words. Do these essays not indeed radiate a unique brilliance? I myself often go to listen to his talks, and in fact have the right and obligation to support the venue. However, because we have been "old friends" for a long time, I would also like to add a few critical words here. First, there is a tendency to overstate the advantages of China, which is contrary to my opinion... Another point... is that reading these essays often makes one feel "so that's how it is." (Omitted below) The author's intention is still to introduce a part of the truth about China to Japanese readers. However, in the present situation, the result will still vary depending on the different readers. This is something that cannot be helped." Finally, I turned to the author's essay "Literary Culture and Life Culture," which served as an introduction. The conclusion was: "Japanese scholars of China have only studied Chinese literature and essays built upon literature. I, however, pay attention to life and want to grasp the culture of life." I also turned to his essay "Convenience Tea," where he said: "I also imitate the Chinese and distribute convenience tea on the streets every year. (Omitted) No matter how fierce the anti-Japanese sentiment, there is no one who does not drink the tea. When one is extremely thirsty, as long as you give them what they want to drink, there is no issue of different nationalities or racial differences. Isn't the reason for rejection and non-use because one has given them something they do not want or are afraid of? What if you give a very thirsty person sticky mud? Someone who asks such a question lacks human understanding." Just as I was about to continue reading, I heard a burst of laughter coming from outside the door. Then, the staff member called out to me, "Mr. Uchiyama is here." He didn't introduce us, but I recognized him because I had been there with Mr. Ya Chen and had seen him before. I walked over to him. As soon as he entered the store, he didn't look elsewhere, but went straight to the back of the bookshelf, which was piled up like a screen, where there were two writing desks (also like accounting desks) and several bamboo chairs lined up (according to Mr. Uchiyama, this was where he, Mr. Lu Xun, and their friends often gathered for casual talks). Although the weather was only cool and not cold, there was already a fire pot burning in the space surrounding the chairs. Mr. Uchiyama was bald, wearing only a woolen sweater on his upper body and a pair of Western-style trousers on his lower body, and he sat down with a smile. I went over to him and introduced myself. He looked at me as if he recognized me, and I then explained my purpose. He laughed again and said, "Excellent, excellent!" After saying this, he looked at me kindly, as if preparing to answer all my questions. I thought for a moment and said, "I have only read a little of your book "View of China," but I already admire it very much. If I read it all, I don't know how much it will broaden my horizons. However, I would like to ask you what observations you have about the Chinese press." He listened carefully, but answered something unrelated: "I have been reading the Shen Bao for nearly twenty years. I don't remember the number of Chinese journalists I have met, but the old journalists from seventeen or eighteen years ago are now very old, or many of them have died and were friends." I continued, "That is indeed an old story. In that case, I would like to ask you where the Uchiyama Bookstore was first established?" He touched his chin, which did not have a long beard, and smiled, "Still at that Weishengli. Twenty years ago, there were not many houses there. The Fumin Hospital was there, and the Guangxuehui was also there. It was like a village surrounded by wilderness. The current Yonganli area was the old Mingqiang Middle School, and there was also a Jesus Church. Around there, a Japanese youth association had also just been established. I was only thirty-one or thirty-two years old then, now I am fifty-two years old. I am four years younger than Mr. Lu Xun, who was fifty-six. It's a pity. I think of many friends from that time: Li Dazhao, Li Hanjun, Chen Duxiu... Now, none of these people can be seen!" He looked lost and wistful for a while. At the same time, he went to find a portrait of Mr. Lu Xun for me and wrote a few words on it. He said, "It's a pity, a real pity that such a person is missing from our casual talk seat." I felt that the atmosphere was too tense, so I switched to another topic: "What do you mean by taking the Chinese name Wu Qishan?" While writing, he said, "The Japanese pronunciation of Uchiyama sounds like 'Wuqi de Mo.' Wu Qishan is a half-Japanese, half-Chinese pronunciation of 'Uchiyama,' and it is also a very correct Chinese name, so I was very happy to adopt it." He immediately found two recent essay drafts for me to read, signed with the name Wu Qishan. I switched to another topic: "Do you like China very much?" "Of course I like it, having lived here for so long, especially Shanghai—what about you?" I found it difficult to answer, but I blurted out, "I love China as much as you cannot forget Japan. But for Shanghai, I feel somewhat differently. I feel that being in Shanghai, I don't feel like I'm in China!" He smiled awkwardly. He paused and said, "According to my observation, from the concrete things that exist in life (that is, in terms of what I call the culture of life), I believe that Shanghai hides China's actual culture of life. Any country will find it impossible to deal with it, but this power still permeates Shanghai! Twenty years of observing Shanghai, I believe this is the case. How many years have you been in Shanghai?" I said uneasily, "Only ten years." "Then I have ten more years than you!" A burst of laughter came from his wide mouth. The light from his near-sighted glasses flashed, indicating that he was shaking his head and very happy. Finally, I asked him if the casual talk sessions were continuing these days. He said, "Twenty years of observation may not be enough until thirty years. So this casual talk cannot be stopped. In addition to the essays collected in the book "A Japanese Person's View of China," there are many more, and perhaps another book will be compiled soon." At this time, I turned to the last page of "View of China" and saw Mr. Lu Xun's letter to the translator, saying: "Mr. Uchiyama's book has a different purpose. The various things he mentions, we ourselves do not notice until they are revealed, so it is interesting, but it would be harmful to be content with this." At this time, his store was about to close, so I said goodbye to Mr. Uchiyama.

Art Scene

Review of "Circus" 204

— Jizhi

The famous American writer A. Sinclair once said: "Art is propaganda." This is indeed a famous saying that gives the most accurate definition of art. We can say that all forms of ideology that are reflected in the superstructure of society due to changes in the infrastructure, whether they express praise, satire, or glorification of the future, have the primary purpose of "propaganda." However, this kind of "propaganda" must be accomplished with mature skills! Especially when it is visualized through theatrical means! It can achieve a universal and powerful effect. Otherwise, due to the poor skills and means, it will not only get the opposite "reaction," but also make "art" itself lose its value.

The film "Circus" demonstrates a new era of work. This not only demonstrates the Soviet Union's creativity and progress towards creating new art, but also tells us that new art has reached maturity.

The Soviet Union occupies a different economic field, and the ideology reflected in the ideological Voloshki has also formed another category. Therefore, in the past in all aspects, especially in art, the attitude of strict criticism and struggle was often taken towards the "legacy of the old": this is an inevitable phenomenon in the process of building a new social system. Now, after several struggles, the Soviet Union has built a considerable foundation in the economic field and has formed a stable state in all aspects of society; similarly, in art, it has also broken away from the tense stage, and has merged the old skills with the new struggle experience to create a new style. The film "Circus" can be said to be a representative work of this new style.

The writer of Mu used the method of symbolism to bring all the unfair phenomena in the world into this film. He also used the new romantic expression method to instill many "justice" and "truth" into the audience through humor. The Germans, "Colonel Knasitz," who symbolize the aggressors in our world, are impatient, narrow-minded, and bullying and humiliating to the weak, the "little black man," symbolizing the weak nations, and the coercion and oppression of the weak woman, "Mary," symbolizing the deprived and oppressed people of the world: All of this can deeply depict our real world. These three archetypes, in their short activities in this film, can be said to have vividly revealed the tyranny of the invaders and the suffering of the oppressed to the audience. On the other hand, the screenwriter also uses various people--Soviets, Georgians, Ukrainians, Jews, Tartars, etc.--for the helpless "little black man," not only because "Knassijue" announced that he was an "illegitimate child" and despised him, but instead, they loved him and passed him around, and used various languages to sing "lullaby" to comfort him. This refutes the "cruelty and inhumanity" of Knassijue, who represents the invaders, and represents the cry of sympathy from the various ethnic groups of the Soviet Union to the weak. The "Circus Manager" said to "Mary" in a humorous tone: "What is the black child afraid of? In the Soviet Union, as long as the child is healthy, it doesn't matter whether it is white, yellow, red, or pink... we want them all." This clearly expresses the Soviet Union's true intention of being international and non-national in a relaxed way.

Its decision is that the characteristic of "Circus" is the appearance of "tap dance" and "leg dance" that have never been seen in Soviet films; in the eyes of ordinary people, or like the past saying that the Soviet Union was capitalist, they thought they were also "leg" with the United States! In fact, it only adopted the old dance form and loaded it with new content, using entertainment to promote "science" and national defense. There are "parachutes" and "flying into the stratosphere", which can be said to be a kind of practical education for the audience, which is different from the general aestheticism of dance.

The author has consistently used the method of symbolism to transform this film into a miniature of the world. At the same time, it also uses several contrasting programs to cross the plot into two sides to symbolize the opposition and competition between the pacifists and the aggressors and all the old forces in the current world. "Knassijue"'s jealousy and sabotage of "Maldnov", and their "close-up" staring at each other on the glass window: This symbolizes the conspiracy of today's aggressors to attack pacifist countries. When "Knassijue" was frantically grabbing the "little black man" from the audience in the circus, he was suddenly stopped by two officers and made him flee in despair: This also symbolizes that only armed forces can stop the aggressor's aggression and brutality. After "Knassijue" and "Mary" performed "Flying to the Moon", Maldnov was moved and immediately wanted to perform "Flying to the Stratosphere". Although he failed because of "Knassijue"'s conspiracy, he was not discouraged, and finally succeeded. This symbolizes the Soviet Union's progressive spirit and competition with capitalism. When the program of "Flying to the Stratosphere" could not be performed, and the old circus manager had to bring out the old trick of "riding a unicycle in 1903" to comfort the audience, although they tried their best to perform it, so that they were "sweating profusely", this outdated trick of "hard work but no reward" could not satisfy the audience's wishes. This also symbolizes that today's world is already the realm of modern people, and everything old should give way.

The author's implication is so profound and meticulous, but the story itself is very simple. And it can establish various different archetypes in this narrow story field. At the same time, with the help of the director, each character in the play can represent a kind of "personality", and in the slow progress of the plot, the audience can slowly understand and understand each unique "personality", and finally get the most profound hit. Except for the role of "Knassijue", because it is necessary to achieve the task of the archetype of "rage"--this kind of "rage", "laughter", "sadness" and other roles are both laborious and difficult to please--the facial expression control is slightly more rigid and facial. Apart from the fact that the roles are more rigid and facialized, the other roles can be said to be able to paint out their characteristics in subtle opportunities.

The structure of the plot is tightly organized and not wasteful because the director uses several clever methods. For example, the part that shows "Mary" traveling all over the world after leaving the United States, and finally arriving at the "Circus" in the Soviet Union, uses the "earth" painted on the train to expand and rotate to become the "ball" in the circus, and the "Eros" imagined by "Maldnov" turned out to be the "Eros" on the satirical painting, and other similar "sketches"; and when "Maldnov" and "Knassijue" looked at each other on the glass window, ice flowers formed on the glass, and the "close-up" of "Knassijue"'s image was isolated. These are all created using the scientific method of "psychological association" and double-exposure. Here, the development of the plot is not cut off, the idea of kinship is destroyed, and the interest in the entire plot is affected because unnecessary "programs" are saved. Director G. Alexandrov can pay attention to these small places, which is indeed helpful to the success of "Circus". However, regarding the "Shi Jiamijing" fighting lions, although this is just to use "humor" to set off this "thrilling" festival, so as to avoid sudden psychological changes in the audience and affect the main plot: But if this "program" is inserted into the "Circus performance", it will appear more natural.

Among the actors, the actress Orlova, who plays "Mary", is indeed a laborious role. She not only has to speak two languages, but also has to sing and dance. Moreover, in the whole process of the play, "Mary's" encounters are extremely complicated: sometimes her life is persecuted, sometimes she is praised for her honor; sometimes she is beaten by the brutal, sometimes she is comforted by her lover; there is bright hope to make her happy, and there is sudden disappointment to make her sad. This role must maintain her unified character in the course of this curve in order to achieve a satisfactory result. And finally, Orlova succeeded.

The role of the manager's daughter "Laya" has appeared in every Soviet film. And the actors who play this type of archetype seem to have a natural "intelligence". She is "innocent", "honest", "careless", and even somewhat "Ah Q" type. Or maybe there are such characters in Soviet society? Perhaps the satire in the drama is "education" for society.

The characters like the "Circus manager" are also common in other Soviet films. The kind of "old man" who is "about to die" is still so lively, humorous, and energetic. I am afraid that only in Soviet society can you find such an old man who has forgotten his age.

In the past few Soviet films, what we have been given are some materials to help us understand the reality of the Soviet Union, or some hints of the future ideals. And "Circus" has gone beyond these scopes and given us many applied theories and skills. We should further learn from these valuable lessons.

Life Guidance

How to Interact with People from Different Countries? 205

— Lu Hui

Shanghai, it is said, has more than 30 nationalities living together with the Chinese. Except for a few high-ranking figures, most salaried people live in lane-style houses or in the new-style row apartments. In one building or one floor of an apartment, there are often people of different nationalities and different provinces. When going in and out, it is often inevitable to have contact with foreigners. At the same time, due to historical reasons and habits, the so-called special areas (the current name of the two concessions, which were called the Foreigner Residential Areas when they were first opened) in Shanghai are clearly divided into national areas. For example, Hongkou is mostly a gathering place for Japanese people, while White Russians gather in the area of Avenue Joffre, and Koreans mostly gather in the area of Route Père Robert. Of course, in the special area, as long as you are a taxpayer who pays taxes according to the regulations, you can choose a residence there at will, without any nationality restrictions. No one can interfere or refuse you. However, therefore, you must consciously or unconsciously use considerable common sense and skills to deal with your left and right neighbors in the residence area. Or, due to occupational reasons, you have to serve in foreign institutions and organizations every day: or, temporary responses and unexpected events make it necessary for you to contact foreigners. Or, later, you become friends. In addition, such as strolling in the park, playing in the ballroom, running along Avenue Joffre and North Sichuan Road, there are more opportunities to contact foreigners.

Let's talk about Japan and the Soviet Union first. People from these two countries are very different in habits and thoughts. But we don't need to care about that: we only ask ourselves how we should treat them. There are relatively few Soviet people in Shanghai. The so-called "Russian" people in Shanghai refer to White Russians. Most of these men work in electrical engineering, patrol the police station, drive buses, check tickets, or work as bodyguards; in addition to opening shops, most of the women work as maids, dancers, or disguised prostitutes. The so-called Russians that we contact in Shanghai are mostly these gentlemen and ladies. When you interact with them, you don't need to praise them for the Five-Year Plan, socialism, or great figures such as Lenin and Gorky. At most, talk about Tolstoy, Chekhov, or the king of songs, Shaliapin, etc. Speaking of Japanese people, they are almost everywhere in the Hongkou area of Shanghai. People in industry and commerce are very polite. According to Japanese people who have lived in Shanghai for a long time: "They are gold worshipers. As long as you have money, they can call you any nice name." However, when you interact with them, you must pay attention to their customs and habits. For example, when you go to a Japanese friend's house, you see that the husband sits and talks or eats with the guests in an arrogant manner, and the wife can only serve cups and pour drinks, add rice and pour tea, and serve with caution like a maid. That is their usual routine. You can't think that this is different from China, and think that your friend is too feudal, so you go to greet the sister-in-law, or repeatedly ask her to eat together before you are willing to move your chopsticks, etc. This is a courtesy in our country, but it will make the sister-in-law embarrassed in their home. It's best if you just ignore her. Also, you must think in advance that you must take off your shoes when you go to a Japanese home. You must pay attention to your feet that have not been washed for a few days and your broken socks in advance. Otherwise, when you get to the time, the wife and young lady of the family will kneel at the door to serve you to take off your shoes according to the rules, wouldn't you be embarrassed?

As for interacting with British people, who are known as gentlemen? Then you must first pay attention to etiquette. This does not mean that you have to dress up in a sophisticated and gorgeous manner; but it means: neat, solemn. Your hair should be combed neatly, and your short beard must be shaved off. If you want to keep a mustache, you must trim the rest neatly. When you go to his house, you must respect the women, you must greet them when you meet them, and you must thank them for any requests. The same as interacting with American women, but the words should be more careful and tactful. Because Americans have always spoken straightforwardly and quickly, while British people are relatively gentle and polite. So some people say: "When you go to a British home, you must first find their bathroom. You must quickly do things like grooming, washing your hands, brushing your clothes, and polishing your leather shoes as soon as you enter the door." This is indeed experienced advice!

It is relatively easy to interact with Americans and French people. But there are differences between the two countries. Most of the current interactions involve women. Americans respect women. For example, when you sit down, men must ask women to sit down first, and you must support them when walking. If two men and one woman walk together, the woman must be allowed to walk in the middle and the two men must support or hold her hand at the same time. If one man walks with two women, then the man should usually support the two women. If two women hold hands, then the man will have to take care of them left and right, serving the two women like a guide.

Garbo's Makeup Talk by Grant Taylor 206

— Heard

The famous Hollywood star, Miss Greta Garbo, says, "Health is our lifeline! It is what provides us with food and clothing!" Originally, in addition to art, what a movie actress needs most urgently are a healthy body and a beautiful appearance, like the peony and its green leaves, supporting each other. A reporter who had traveled to Hollywood once asked this mysterious woman, Garbo, "How can one maintain health for a long time?" According to her, "Go to bed early and wake up early every day, sleeping for eight hours is appropriate. Take a bath every day for ten minutes, using lukewarm water with a little milk and salt, and after the bath, apply a beauty lotion all over the body until it turns rosy. In my experience, golf is the most suitable exercise, or riding a bicycle. Because the beauty of the face is entirely created by the skin and flesh, which are nourished by blood, and blood is the crystallization of diet, its master is still nutrition, so I pay great attention to diet, the outline of which is as follows: (1) Choose vegetables rich in protein, and do not eat too much fatty food, for fear of making you fat easily. (2) Drink a glass of fresh milk every morning and afternoon. (3) Do not drink strong tea or smoke cigarettes. (4) Eat a small amount of fruit after meals to maintain cleanliness in the stomach and intestines, and avoid indigestion and all internal diseases.

As for makeup, its quality entirely depends on personal experience and the quality of the makeup and beauty products chosen. However, I can offer a few small suggestions:

(1) The best time for makeup is after getting up in the morning and after meals. Before makeup, put aside all worries, as a restless mood can greatly affect beauty! When applying powder, first apply Cartose oil all over the face, as it can make it even and prevent the face from being attacked by lead in the powder, which can cause spots. (2) The circles around the eyes should be light black, as dark ones appear unnatural. (3) Rouge should be red during the day and yellow in the evening, while lipstick should be dark red both day and night. (4) Avoid applying any perfume to the face, as it contains alcohol, which is very irritating and harmful to the skin. (5) At night when going to bed, apply a little fatty oil to the face to make the skin white and tender. If spots or wrinkles appear on the face, go to a beauty hospital for surgery immediately to prevent them from growing. And I think every movie star should know a familiar beauty doctor to maintain her youth."

At the same time, if your female relative is with a French male friend, you may find it uncomfortable, and your female relatives may feel that he is impolite. In fact, this is just the habit of French friends, and they, like her, have no bad intentions. Therefore, special attention should be paid to this point. It is said that in Paris, there are actually social circles where people exchange wives for daily life, but that is a very small number of cases. The French do indeed take a calm view of entanglements between men and women, but in other people's countries, they also value friendship and politeness.

They are both very dedicated to their duties and are very enthusiastic and careful to everyone in their duties. Amateur Studies

How to Learn Sketching 207

— Dun

Painting is indeed interesting, especially "sketching." Because the materials are readily available, as long as you have a keen eye and a careful mind, and a clear judgment of beauty and ugliness, you can depict anything, and what you depict can become a beautiful work.

"Sketching" is generally divided into two types: one is "still life sketching" and the other is "landscape sketching." Still life sketching is a necessary step for those who learn to paint. Beginners always start by drawing plaster models. First, we prepare a triangular wooden frame, the height of which is equal to the chest when standing. Make several symmetrical holes on the left and right sides of the two feet in front of the wooden frame, and then prepare a large piece of thick paper or a thin piece of wood, insert wooden pillars into the holes in the feet, and hold up the thick paper or thin piece. Its position must be suitable for the line of sight of the eyes. What we want to depict can be hung on the opposite wall or placed on a high platform on the opposite side; this position cannot be arbitrarily placed. Beginners must place the drawing materials in a place with light coming from one side, that is, a place with horizontal light; because in this kind of light, it is easy to distinguish the light and dark of the object and feel the "three-dimensionality" and "distance" of the object. Once this position is arranged properly, then start painting: use nails to nail the drawing paper (usually called drawing paper) on the thick paper or thin board. If you are a beginner, directly use charcoal to draw the drawing materials in front of you on the paper. But is it considered a "masterpiece" if you just draw it like this? No, if you meticulously describe it like this, it simply becomes a rigid "explanatory diagram." Painting is like writing an article, you must give a "soul" to your work: that is, before applying charcoal to the drawing paper, you must carefully observe the shape, light and dark, and color of each part of the drawing material, and deeply imprint it on your brain, and then make a real description. Only by first understanding the overall posture and interest of the drawing material can you discover its charm in the overall composition of the color, light and dark, and lines of the object. This kind of "discovery" seems very abstract, but in fact, as long as you practice more and observe more, you will gain it unintentionally.

If the material taken is relatively complicated and cannot be finished in a short period of time, you can put it down and continue the next day. However, the painting time each time must be fixed at the same time. If the first time is started in the morning, you must continue to work in the morning from then on; because the light is different in the morning and afternoon, and the light and dark shown on the object will naturally be different; this does not matter much to people with a foundation in painting; but for beginners, there will be difficulties because the same drawing material will show various different phenomena due to different light.

Secondly, if you want to color, in addition to the above points, you must also pay attention to the color tone of the drawing material. If it is a plaster statue or porcelain, etc., because it is white itself, it will be difficult to show the concavity and convexity of the object if it is placed on a white background. Therefore, the color of the drawing material and the background must be very clear and harmonious; for example, if you want to draw a white porcelain pot with tangerines and apples in it, in order to show its color, you can use a light blue (that is, lake blue) cloth as a lining in the back, so you can get a vivid impression of the color of each object.

For paintings that need to be colored, first use charcoal to draw the general outline on drawing paper or canvas according to an appropriate composition. After drawing, gently sweep away the heavy ash of the charcoal; (those with a painting foundation often do not use charcoal, but directly use an oil painting brush to dip in color and draw the outline) then paint it stroke by stroke according to the color of the original object. In purple drawing (only using charcoal to draw without coloring), it is often natural to use charcoal to describe the concentration of light or shadows, but in the description of color, it is necessary to express these parts with the contrast of color tones.

Whether it is monochrome drawing or color description, in addition to paying attention to "light and dark" and "color," the proportions of each part of the object cannot be ignored at all. We often see strange phenomena in advertisements on the market, such as a hat worn on the chest or arms longer than the legs, which are all due to not paying attention to the proportions of each part of the object. Learning painting must learn "perspective," which is to correct this kind of error, but if we don't have much time to study this step, when we paint, we use the pen in our hand as a ruler to roughly measure each part of the object. When measuring, there is no need to run close and pick up the object to measure it. We just stand far away, squint one eye, raise the pen, look over, and see how many parts of the pen each part occupies, and then compare it with each part of our spirit.

After having sufficient training in still life sketching, you can learn "landscape sketching."

The most difficult thing in landscape sketching is that the light and dark are not easy to grasp, because landscape sketching is mostly outdoors, and the light and dark outdoors are abnormally complex, but if you have a considerable foundation in still life sketching, this kind of difficulty is still easy to avoid.

Outdoors, the sunlight is constantly moving, so the light and dark parts or silhouettes shown on the famous things are also moving all the time. For example, the shadow of a tree is here at first sight, and in an instant, it has stretched to the other side. Therefore, the person who sketches must describe it as much as possible within the period when the scenery has not changed much. If you feel that the scenery is too different from when you first came, it is not suitable to continue, it is better to stop immediately and come to work again at the same time tomorrow, otherwise, the whole painting will be changed here and there, and it will fall into a situation where it is all worthless.

If you go to a place and can't decide which part to take as a drawing material for a while, then you can use a pencil to roughly sketch several parts of what you see in the sketchbook (there are special ones for sale) in advance. By comparing the parts with each other, you can decide which one you want to take. With the material, then, like still life sketching, first understand the structure of the part to be described. For example, there is a small stream in that part, and there are a few sparse trees on one side of the stream, with the shadows of the trees quietly reflected in the water, and the other side is full of fluffy green grass, and in front is a wide field, and in the farthest place (distant view) there are smoky forests... To describe this, first define a horizon line on the drawing paper or canvas to determine the position of the distant view, and then use this horizon line as a starting point to arrange the positions of the foreground and the main objects, such as trees, streams, and stream banks. After deciding, first draw the general outline. If coloring, first dye the color of the sky, and then paint the middle view and distant view in order. Naturally, when drawing these, you must not only pay attention to the shape of the objects, but also pay attention to the contrast between light and dark and the difference in the distance of each scene at all times. Otherwise, all the objects will stick together, and the three-dimensional shape will not be shown.

When sketching in strong sunlight, the screen must be protected from direct sunlight. In strong sunlight, a sketching umbrella can be used and inserted next to the easel (use the easel for still life sketching) to shield the sunlight. If you don't use an umbrella, you can borrow the shelter of the leaves under the shade of a tree. If there is strong sunlight in front of the painting or strong light reflected from the ground, it is not suitable for sketching and should be avoided. Also, if there is a strong wind and the easel is not stable, you can find a stone and hang it in the middle of the three feet to prevent the easel from being blown over by the wind by relying on the force of the center of gravity.

What has been said above is just a general outline of sketching. This is originally a special subject that requires a long time to study. However, if we know a little bit about the doorway and practice diligently, we will also have excellent results. For example, Millet in France was so poor that he couldn't even afford charcoal and drawing paper, where would he have the money to go to school to listen to "Perspective" and "Painting Theory"? However, his works "Evening Bell," "Gleaners," and "Sheep Flock," painted with pitiful coal ash and waste paper, have become priceless treasures to this day.

International Intelligence

The Chemical Warfare Preparations of the Great Powers 208

— Bi Jia

As everyone knows, chemical weapons such as poison gas, smoke bombs, and incendiary bombs were actually used in the World War of 1914-18. After the war, the great powers worked even harder to prepare for chemical warfare. Their military experts and scientists were always publicizing the great role of chemical weapons and were always working hard to invent new killing weapons. General Fuller of England once said: "The shells 'die' as soon as they fall on the ground; while the micro-molecules of chemical substances, when released, can continue to 'survive'. Whether on the ground or underground, even after a few days, it will give everything a terrible blow." General De Ve of Italy also pointed out that chemical weapons can be sent to extremely far places and have a great effect, saying that they can not only attack the enemy's front, but also harass its rear, and thus assert that the emergence of airborne chemical weapons will change all forms of warfare. In this way, the importance of the task played by chemical weapons in the upcoming world war can be imagined.

The great powers' preparations for chemical warfare are first manifested in the chemical industry. After the war, based on the experience of the application of chemical weapons, the imperialist powers all worked hard to create and develop chemical industry departments directly related to the production of chemical weapons. These industrial sectors mainly produce chlorine, arsenic, sulfur, rayon, nitrogen, aniline dyes, and other chemical drugs. In recent years, due to the increasing tension in the world situation, the production capacity of chemicals by the imperialist powers has shown an alarming increase. For example, the possible production capacity of chlorine in the great powers recently is shown as follows——

United States 600,000 tons

France 100,000 tons

Japan 130,000 tons

Germany 150,000 tons

England 100,000 tons

Poland 100,000 tons

However, the actual production volume of chlorine in various countries showed the following state——

United States 300,000 tons

France 70-75,000 tons

Japan 70-80,000 tons

Germany 100-35,000 tons

England 70-75,000 tons

Poland 30-40,000 tons

In this way, if the chlorine production capacity of the great powers is compared with their actual production volume (especially the consumption volume), then the imbalance can be clearly seen. This alarming imbalance fully illustrates the efforts of the great powers in the production and preparation of chlorine.

Among the great powers, the most effort in the development of the chemical industry has been made by Japan in the East and Germany in the West. In Japan, the development of the rayon industry has first attracted the attention of the world. According to the survey, in the recent three years, the Japanese rayon industry has
